Ticket Prices 168

The prices for one-way through-tickets from Shanghai, Nanjing, and Hankow to Kuling are as follows, divided into First Class A, First Class B, Official Cabin, and Room Cabin categories: Shanghai to Kuling, China Merchants Steam Navigation Company: First Class A is 49 yuan and 31 yuan, Official Cabin is 21.8 yuan and 18 yuan, Room Cabin is 14.4 yuan and 14 yuan; Jardine Matheson: First Class A is 55 yuan, First Class B is 40 yuan, Official Cabin is 20 yuan, Room Cabin is 15 yuan; Butterfield & Swire: First Class A is 45 yuan, Official Cabin is 20 yuan, Room Cabin is 15 yuan (all prices include steamer, bus, and mountain sedan chair). At the same time, China Travel Service, in order to provide thorough service and extra comfort for passengers, has set up information centers with guesthouses at both the Jiujiang Garden Hotel and the Lianhua Cave office. Booking of cabins, buses from Jiujiang to Lianhua Cave, and sedan chairs for climbing the mountain from Lianhua Cave, as well as luggage transport directly to mountain residences, can all be arranged. Designated personnel are dispatched to provide assistance along the way.

Baggage Fees 169

(1) Shanghai to Kuling Express: 2.88 yuan per load, up to 55 catties; Slow: 2.78 yuan per item, up to 100 catties; 3.31 yuan for 100 to 150 catties; 3.56 yuan for 150 to 200 catties. (2) Nanjing to Kuling Express: 2.68 yuan per load, up to 55 catties; Slow: 2.58 yuan per item, up to 100 catties; 3.16 yuan for 100 to 150 catties; 3.36 yuan for 150 to 200 catties. (3) Hankow to Kuling Express: 2.88 yuan per load, up to 55 catties; Slow: 2.78 yuan per item, up to 100 catties; 3.31 yuan for 100 to 150 catties; 3.56 yuan for 150 to 200 catties. (The above express and slow services include the Lushan Administration's police donation of 8 fen per 100 catties, as well as dock fees in Shanghai, Jiujiang, Nanchang, Hankow, etc.)

Buses and Mountain Sedan Chairs 170

(1) Bus: The distance between Jiujiang and Lianhua Cave is 24 li, and the journey takes about half an hour. There are two types of buses, large and small, with a fare of 1.8 yuan per person (including taxes and fees). Children under 12 are charged half price. If chartering a bus, a full ten tickets must be purchased for a large bus and a full four tickets must be purchased for a small bus. (2) Mountain Sedan Chair: The distance between Lianhua Cave and Kuling is 20 li. All sedan chairs are carried by four chair carriers, and the fare is 3.2 yuan per chair (including police donation and canopy). If the passenger weighs over 160 pounds, two additional chair carriers are required. If the passenger weighs over 240 pounds, four additional chair carriers are required. Each additional chair carrier is charged an additional 0.7 yuan. The ascent takes approximately four hours, and the descent takes approximately two hours. If using a sleeping sedan chair, an additional 0.5 yuan is charged per ride. Tips for chair carriers are 0.2 yuan each for wine. If encountering rain or snow, or traveling at night, or in areas such as Lulin and Huanglong, each chair carrier is charged an additional 0.1 yuan.

Chen Tongfu, Employee of Fuhua Pharmacy, Commits Suicide News of Qin Lizhai's Wife's Suicide Found Near His Body 171

Chen Tongfu, a native of Ningbo, 33 years old, and an employee of Fuhua Pharmacy located at No. 231 Carter Road, recently felt financially strained. He suddenly developed suicidal thoughts a few days ago and secretly took poison to end his life. Chen lived on the third floor of the pharmacy. This morning, a colleague, Fu Youlun, noticed that it was already late in the morning, but Chen had not yet gotten up. So, he went to check on him and discovered that Chen was groaning in bed. He immediately reported to the Xinzha Police Station, who dispatched detectives to investigate. They took Chen to Renji Hospital, but the treatment was ineffective, and he soon died. A newspaper clipping about the suicide of Qin Lizhai's wife and children, as well as a suicide note, were found near his body. This proves that his suicidal thoughts had been brewing for some time. The body was transported to the Fei Lun Road morgue. Yesterday morning, Guo Wei, a prosecutor appointed by the First Special District Local Court, along with forensic doctor Zhang Yan and clerk Wang Zuyi, arrived at the morgue to examine the body. After questioning, Chen Xifang, the deceased's brother, who resides at No. 76 Dongxinqiao and runs a pharmacy, testified that "the deceased was my younger brother. He has always been in severe financial distress. Therefore, this sudden suicide must be due to this." He also requested to claim the body. After reviewing the testimony, Mr. Guo ruled that Chen Tongfu, male, had indeed died from taking poison before his death, and authorized the release of the body to his brother, Chen Xifang, for burial.

New Cocoons from Jiangsu and Zhejiang Enter the Market Prices of Chinese Raw Silk in European and American Markets Fall to Unprecedented Low Levels Thus, Cocoon Prices Follow Suit, Impacting Rural Areas 172

China's silk industry has been affected by the dumping of Japanese silk in European and American markets, causing market prices to plummet. Silk mills in Jiangsu and Zhejiang have mostly shut down. Now, new cocoons have begun to enter the market, and cocoon prices have fallen, severely impacting the livelihoods of farmers. Details are as follows:

New Cocoons Enter the Market 173

Due to climate conditions, the silkworms in Jiangsu's Wuxi, Liyang, and other areas are doing very well. Zhejiang's Shengxian, Haining, and other areas have been slightly affected. Today, the new cocoons in Shaoxing and Shengxian, Zhejiang, are priced at 25 yuan per 100 catties for the native Donggao variety. Those in Changan, Haining, are scheduled to enter the market today. Those in Jiaxing and Pinghu are expected to enter around the 27th or 28th of this month, and those in Hangzhou, Huzhou, and other areas are expected to enter at the end of this month. Those in Liyang, Jiangsu, are expected to enter at the end of this month, and those in Wuxi are expected to enter at the beginning of next month. As for market prices, although they vary from place to place, the native variety is generally priced at 20 to 30 yuan per 100 catties, and the improved variety is priced at 25 to 35 yuan per 100 catties.

Decline in Exports 174

Chinese raw silk is mainly used for foreign trade. Since European and American markets have been affected by the dumping of Japanese silk, causing market prices to plummet, the silk reeled by various mills has incurred heavy losses. The current price of standard Chinese raw silk is below 500 yuan per dan, an unprecedented low. Furthermore, there are no large-scale transactions. The market in Shanghai is barely maintaining itself. Less than one-tenth of the cocoon merchants have started reeling silk, and they are operating intermittently. Considering the current market price of new cocoons and the silk market in Europe and America, it is still difficult to make a profit from collecting cocoons and reeling silk this spring. Silk merchants generally hope that Chinese raw silk will improve.

Impact on Rural Areas 175

After the new cocoons enter the market, silk merchants who collect cocoons urgently try to sell them and inevitably reel silk. Therefore, silk mills in Jiangsu and Zhejiang are about to resume operations. In Shanghai, it is currently expected that about 30 mills can start operating. However, based on the current market price of new cocoons this spring, farmers who raise silkworms will not be able to make a profit even if they have a good harvest. If they are slightly less fortunate, they will inevitably suffer losses. Therefore, the impact on the rural economy is significant.

Chen A'fa Knifes Adulterer and Adulteress Adulterer Gao Yihe Dies Adulteress Severely Injured in Lower Body 176

Chen A'fa, a 25-year-old native of Wuxi and a chauffeur by trade, lived at No. 259 Wuding Road. He married a woman named Lu, a 19-year-old native of Suzhou. The two were initially deeply in love. However, Chen's work kept him away from home. The young Lu, unaccustomed to sleeping alone, would go out to play when her husband was away. A man named Gao Yihe, a 21-year-old native of Taizhou who was not yet married and spent his days loitering, saw Lu and was struck by her beauty. He tried every means to seduce her, and Lu also flirted with him. Soon, they became acquainted, felt deeply in love with each other, and used inns as places for their secret rendezvous. Chen A'fa, Lu's husband, heard about this but, unable to obtain solid proof, decided that moving would be a good idea. So, he moved his home to No. 49 Yongji Lane, Xinzha Road, hoping to sever the two parties' relationship. However, Lu was infatuated with her lover. On the night before last, while Chen A'fa was away at work, she summoned Gao to her home for a secret rendezvous. Unexpectedly, Chen discovered this and suddenly returned home around 4:00 AM yesterday morning. He found the adulterer and adulteress sound asleep. Enraged by the sight, Chen A'fa grabbed a kitchen knife from the table and slashed wildly at Gao's legs and Lu's lower body. The two were unable to resist and were both injured. Their cries for help attracted neighbors, who rushed over and found the man and woman lying in pools of blood. They immediately called the police, who arrested Chen and took him to the Xinzha Police Station. The injured man and woman were transported to the hospital for treatment. However, Gao died in the hospital around 11:00 AM yesterday due to his severe injuries. His body was immediately transported to the morgue for examination. Lu's lower body was also severely injured, and her life is in danger.

Trial of Trafficking of La Mei Zhang Zhou's Search for Daughter Successful Matchmaker Suspected of Profiteering 177

Zhang Zhou's daughter, Zhang Lamei, a 17-year-old resident of No. 357 Tangqiao, Pudong, was trafficked out last October. Wu Quanjin and Wang Yande sold her to Gong Fushan of Beicai Town, Pudong, as a daughter-in-law for 130 yuan. This year, Zhang Zhou found her and reported to the police. Wu Quanjin, Wang Yande, and others were arrested and brought to the local court. Prosecutor Yang An filed a public indictment against them for violating morality and family laws. Yesterday, Judge Zhang Peiming opened the court to hear the case. Wu Quanjin testified: "I am from Shanghai, residing at No. 44 Jianyu Lane, Haichao Temple. I am a tailor." Judge asked: "Do you know Xing Guisheng?" Wu answered: "I don't know him." Judge asked: "Do you know Gong Fushan?" Wu answered: "I don't know him. I only know Fang A'mei." Judge asked: "Do you know Yang A'bing?" Wu answered: "I don't know him." Judge asked: "Do you know Wang Yande?" Wu answered: "I know him." Judge asked: "You acted as a matchmaker for a woman sold to Gong Fushan?" Wu answered: "Wang Yande begged me, saying that there was a young lady who had been expelled by her relatives for adultery, and her mother and sister asked for a way to save her life. Later, my friend Fang A'mei happened to be at my place, and we talked about it. Fang acted as a matchmaker for Gong A'fu. The total bride price was 130 yuan, and I only received a matchmaker fee of 5 yuan." Judge asked: "Where was the money exchanged?" Wu answered: "At my home. Fang A'mei gave it to me and I gave it to Wang Yande." At this point, the Judge asked Wang Yande to testify: "I am 40 years old, from Shengxian, residing at No. 16 Shachang Street, and I am a tailor. I do not know Zhang Lamei. Xing Guitang said that there was a 17-year-old girl who had been expelled by her relatives, and her mother had remarried. This girl was acting as a matchmaker. Her mother could come to the court. We were chatting idly, not seriously. Wu Quanjin's friend, Yan A'mei, happened to be there and said that her relative wanted to go and talk about it. After several days, she claimed success, but we had to meet face-to-face and talk. We didn't want to pursue it further." Judge asked: "Have you seen her sister and mother?" Wu answered: "I saw them at the Dongjiadu teahouse. The bride price was 130 yuan, and I received a matchmaker fee of 5 yuan." Judge asked: "Where is Xing Guitang?" Wu answered: "Xing's residence on Dalianwan Road. I didn't know I would encounter this slippery matter." Gong Fushan testified: "I am 53 years old, from Nanhui, residing in Beicai Town, and I am a farmer. Fang A'mei acted as the matchmaker for Zhang Lamei. They sent her on a ship, brought her back, and married her to my son. We wrote a marriage certificate, saying that she was from the Yang family of Yangsiqiao. I do not recognize the others at all." Zhang Lamei testified: "I am 17 years old, from Shanghai, residing in Tangqiao, Pudong. On October 21st of last year, Yang A'bing, who used to be a tenant in my home, tricked me into going out to play. I called Yang 'maternal uncle.' Unexpectedly, he took me to his home at No. 11 Zhangjia Lane, where he raped me. Then, he tricked me into buying foreign cloth. He sent me to Dongjiadu and excused himself to go to the bathroom, never to return. When the ship set sail, I cried and made a fuss, but Gong took me away." Zhang Zhou testified: "I am 45 years old. Zhang Lamei is my daughter. After she was trafficked, Mr. Wang, a director of Tangqiao, said to go and take a look at Gong Fushan's home in Beicai. I went and recognized her. My daughter cried loudly, so I knew about this." At this point, the judge ordered Wang Yande to identify the woman in the courtroom. Judge asked: "Do you recognize her?" Wu said that he met her in Yizhichun. The woman said that she recognized him from a previous encounter. At this point, Fang A'mei testified: "I only recognize Wu Quanjin as the matchmaker. The rest is roughly the same." At this point, the judge ordered that the defendants be sent back into custody for further questioning.

China Merchants Bureau Rents Various Ships from Da Zhen Company, the Handover Started Yesterday with a Term of Eight Months; Yong Ping and Yong An Sail to Shanghai and Fujian; Yong Ji Sails to Lao Yao 180

The state-run China Merchants Bureau has leased the Yong Ping, Yong An, and Yong Ji ships from Da Zhen Navigation Company to operate on the Shanghai-Fuzhou line and the Shanghai-Lao Yao line. After the contract was signed, the handover of the ships started yesterday for a term of eight months. The details are recorded as follows:

Impact of Joint Transportation 181

The Yong Ping ship of Da Zhen Navigation Company has a total tonnage of 1,422 tons, and the Yong An has the same total tonnage as the Yong Ping. The Yong Ji has a total tonnage of 1,847 tons. It specializes in the Shanghai line. Since the implementation of joint transportation between the Longhai Railway and the China Merchants Bureau, all joint transportation goods have been loaded and unloaded at the Sun Jia Shan Wharf in Lao Yao. Therefore, the business of Da Zhen Company's Da Pu Wharf has been affected by the joint transportation, so it reduced the water freight to compete with it, but it was ultimately ineffective. There were rumors that the China Merchants Bureau was buying Da Zhen Company, but Da Zhen Company strongly denied it.

Leasing to China Merchants 182

In view of the reduction of cargo at Haizhou Da Pu Wharf and the upcoming completion of the new wharves in Lao Yao and Lian Yun Gang, the Da Zhen Company realized that in the future, the cargo of the Longhai Railway will inevitably be concentrated in Lian Yun Gang. Although the Ministry of Communications and the Ministry of Railways have approved the company to participate in joint transportation, the Yong Ping and Yong An are shallow-water ships and are not suitable for sailing in Lian Yun Gang. Therefore, Feng Zhen Duo, the manager of the company, contacted Liu Hong Sheng, the general manager of the China Merchants Bureau, and leased all three ships, Yong Ping, Yong An, and Yong Ji, to the China Merchants Bureau. A formal contract has been signed for a term of eight months.

Changing to Sail to Shanghai and Fujian 183

The China Merchants Bureau originally dispatched the Tai Shun ship to operate on the Shanghai-Fuzhou line. Because the ship has a total tonnage of 1,962 tons, and the Min River above Mawei is shallow, it cannot sail and can only dock at Luoxing Tower in Mawei, and then use barges to transfer to Fuzhou Provincial City. After the lease, it was decided to dispatch the Yong Ping and Yong An to operate on the Shanghai-Fuzhou line. Because they are shallow-water ships, they can directly reach Fuzhou Provincial City. However, the Yong Ji ship has a larger tonnage and is dispatched between Shanghai and Lao Yao to load joint transportation goods. The Tai Shun ship, which originally sailed on the Shanghai-Fuzhou line, has been changed to the Shanghai-Tianjin line.

Starting the Handover 184

After the ships of Da Zhen Company were leased to the China Merchants Bureau, all the crew members and compradors remained the same, and the expenses of the comprador on the ship were also handled as usual. The Yong Ping ship has been handed over to the China Merchants Bureau today. The shipowner held a letter from Da Zhen Company and went to the China Merchants Bureau this morning to receive the Yong Ping ship. It is scheduled to sail to Fuzhou for the first time tomorrow. As for the Yong An and Yong Ji ships, they will be handed over to the China Merchants Bureau upon their return to Shanghai.

Da Zhen's Plan 185

The reason why Da Zhen Company leased all of its ships to the China Merchants Bureau this time is due to business reasons. However, the China Merchants Bureau happened to need shallow-water ships due to the problem of the Shanghai-Fuzhou line, so the deal was concluded. It is heard that the monthly rent is about more than 20,000 yuan. Da Zhen Company will not give up the Shanghai-Lao Yao line. After the establishment of the Joint Office for Joint Transportation between State-owned and Private Sectors, it will purchase two more ships ranging from 4,000 to 5,000 tons to operate on the Shanghai-Lao Yao line to load joint transportation goods. After the expiration of the Yong Ping and other two ships, it will be recovered for its own use, and the route will depend on future business.

The Garden Hotel on Qingyang Port: A New Construction on the Jinghu, Huhangyong Roads, the Hostel and Garden Are Very Convenient for Rest and Recreation 186

The Jinghu, Huhangyong Railway Administration, in view of the fact that people in Shanghai are living in a noisy environment and urgently need a place to cultivate their emotions and purify their nature in order to regulate their lives, found that the Qingyang Port area near Kunshan has a quiet scenery, free from dust, and is very close to Shanghai, with convenient transportation. It is very suitable for arranging recreational places. It sent personnel to find a Jiang family garden property on the edge of Qingyang Port, which was very suitable. Therefore, it was rented and opened as a garden hotel, so that people in Shanghai can rest and visit there at any time. The place has ancient trees, tall bamboos, strange rocks and exotic flowers, and pavilions are reflected in the flowers and trees, the grass is as green as a carpet, and the waves are as smooth as a mirror. Being in it is like entering a painting. Here you can have a picnic on the ground, fish with a rod, or drive a small boat to float in the clear water, which is enough to broaden your mind and cultivate your spirit. Regarding the accommodation and food for travelers, the hotel is clean and well-equipped, and the service is attentive, and the fees are very low. This kind of facility is really no different from opening a paradise for people in Shanghai. Those who want to cultivate their body and mind and visit the boat race should not miss it).

Revision of the Huhangyong Railway; Method of Commission for Transportation of Tea Chests 187

Central News Agency reports that tea chests are one of the major transportation items on the Huhangyong line. More than 200,000 chests are transported to Shanghai by rail every year, mostly shipped from Anhui Province to the Zhakou, loaded on trains and transported to Shanghai. In order to encourage merchants to transport, the bureau previously stipulated a special commission method in the appendix to the freight car transportation rules of the Huhangyong line (officially recognized transshipment companies or private merchants who have paid a railway deposit of 1,700 yuan, and whose total annual shipment of tea chests exceeds 100,000 chests, can enjoy a 3% commission). The transportation of this tea chest has always been undertaken exclusively by Maoshuntai Company. Although the company voluntarily cancelled the official recognition and took back the deposit last year, it did not actually close down. Therefore, the tea chests last year were still transported by the company, and the total transportation volume still exceeded the prescribed amount. However, because the deposit has been taken back, it cannot enjoy the commission benefits according to the regulations. In order to prevent water transport competition, the Traffic Department intends to appropriately increase the commission and revise the previous method to the effect that all merchants who load tea chests at Zhakou, Nanxing, Hangzhou, Genshanmen, and Gongchen stations on the Huhangyong line and transport them directly to Shangbei, Shangnan, and Rihui Port, and who have first registered the brand name with the railway and paid a tea chest transportation deposit of 500 yuan, will be given a special commission at the end of the year according to the following standards. However, those who have received a special commission will no longer enjoy the general commission. The special commission stipulates that for annual transportation exceeding 50,000 chests, the commission is 2.5%; for exceeding 100,000 chests, the commission is 3%; for exceeding 150,000 chests, the commission is 3.5%; for exceeding 200,000 chests, the commission is 4%; and for exceeding 250,000 chests, the commission is 5%. This has been approved by the bureau.

Dagong News reports that after the British-American Tobacco Company in Pudong announced the closure of the old factory on the 12th of this month, more than 3,000 male and female workers suddenly became unemployed. The Cigarette Workers' Union of the Fifth District convened representatives from the new and old factories to discuss the matter. It was decided that in order to urge the factory to realize the situation, the workers of the new factory would all go on strike from last Thursday to provide assistance. However, most of the workers in the factory had been taking turns to rest in the past few days. Yesterday, all of them went to work. More than 4,000 male and female workers in the leaf room, workshop, tin packaging room, printing department, pattern-making room, box room, tin foil room, machine room, coppersmith room, and lead room of the new factory went to the factory as usual at 6:00 AM, but after entering the factory, they all went on strike. In the afternoon, the factory side was deeply afraid of causing trouble, so it closed the factory door, so the workers did not enter the factory, but no incidents occurred.

Dispatching Police for Prevention 194

The Director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, Wen Hongen, reported that the workers of the new factory went on strike yesterday morning. He was deeply afraid that the large number of people would cause accidents, so he ordered Zhang Mingqin, the Director of the Public Security Bureau of the Third District, to send police to maintain order. After receiving the order, Director Zhang, in addition to ordering the police stationed in the factory to pay attention at any time, personally led more than 20 police officers to suppress the incident at 6:00 AM yesterday. Shi Keshi, the captain of the Third Squadron of the Pudong Police Brigade, also led a small team of police officers to assist. It was not until 12:00 noon that they were withdrawn separately.

The Crew Members of the Jinglong Ship Who Were Rescued Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday; All the Cargo Was Lost, Totaling About 140,000 Yuan; Rescue Was Difficult, and the Shipowner Was Buried on Guyu 203

The crew members of the Jinglong ship of the Hengkang Shipping Company, who were rescued after hitting a reef in the port of Xiamen, have arrived in Shanghai. The Russian shipowner who committed suicide has been buried on Gulangyu. All the cargo was lost, and the rescue of the ship was difficult. The details are recorded below:

All Cargo Lost 204

The Jinglong ship was loaded with 1,300 tons of food, flour, groceries, etc. After hitting the reef, the Xiamen Customs sent a ship to unload and store them in the customs warehouse. However, because all the cargo had been soaked in water, the food and flour had fermented. Except for the cargo on the deck, which was unloaded by the customs, the remaining cargo in the hold has now stopped unloading, because the cargo is useless and the unloading cost is too uneconomical, so it has been abandoned. The total loss of cargo is about 140,000 yuan.

Difficult to Rescue 205

After the Jinglong ship hit the reef, the Ship Insurance Association telegraphed Xiamen Dock to estimate the cost of rescue. The ship is still stranded on the reef. Because the bottom of the ship has been damaged, the rescue is quite difficult. According to the dock report, it will have to wait for a very high tide or flood to rescue it. The Xiamen Customs has sent a small steamship to station beside the ship. If it escapes danger, the loss will not be worth it.

Crew Arrived in Shanghai 206

All the crew members who were rescued were initially settled by the Xiamen agent. Now, because the Jinglong ship cannot be rescued for a while, they took the Fuping ship from Xiamen to Shanghai yesterday and reported to Hengkang Company. As for the Russian shipowner who committed suicide, he has been buried on Gulangyu. All expenses were advanced by the Russian Consul in Xiamen.

Tao Jia Yao v. Gao Xiao Chen Injury Case: Tao Unable to Climb Stairs Due to Serious Injury, Next Trial Changed to Downstairs 211

The case of former Jiangxi Governor Tao Jia Yao, represented by lawyers Yan Luo Jia Heng, Wang Zao Shi, and Li Guo Zhen, filing a complaint with the Criminal Court of the Second Special District Local Court, accusing Gao Xiao Chen of injury and requesting investigation and punishment according to Article 295 of the Criminal Law, etc., has been repeatedly reported in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, another summons was received. The plaintiff, Tao Jia Yao, was still unable to appear in court due to his injuries. The defendant, Gao Xiao Chen, arrived with his defense lawyer. The court immediately questioned witness Luo Rui Xiu, who stated, "I work in the magistrate's office on the upper floor of this court. On the afternoon of the third of this month, after the adjournment of Gao Xiao Chen's lawsuit against Tao Jia Yao, I was standing at the office door when I suddenly saw a tall man say to Tao Jia Yao, 'You shouldn't have said bad things about me in court, I will beat you to death, you bastard,' etc. As for the details of the beating, I did not see them." Witness Guo Shang Yun stated, "I work as a court guard in this court. On the day the Gao Tao lawsuit adjourned, I only heard someone shouting, 'Don't hit, don't hit.' The official asked if he saw the beating. Guo replied that he did not see it. Afterwards, in the lawyers' lounge, I saw Tao Jia Yao vomit two mouthfuls of blood, and I don't know anything else." The official then asked the plaintiff's representative lawyer whether the plaintiff could personally appear in court. Lawyer Luo replied, "Although the plaintiff can move to the court, he cannot climb the stairs. I request that the next hearing be changed to the downstairs courtroom, so that the plaintiff can appear in court." Magistrate Wu Fang Lian then approved the postponement to this Thursday (the 24th) for trial in Criminal Court Eight. After the order was given, the court was adjourned.

Ministry of Communications Orders Seafarers to Apply for Certificates Within a Time Limit; Fourth Seafarer Examination Scheduled 212

The fourth seafarer qualification examination is scheduled to be held on July 27th. The Ministry of Communications has instructed the Navigation Bureau to notify all shipping companies. The Ministry of Communications also stated that a small number of seafarers have not yet applied for certificates, which violates the ministry's order, and has again ordered strict compliance, setting the end of June as the deadline. Those who still do not have certificates by the deadline will have their duties suspended. The details are explored and recorded below:

Fourth Examination 213

The seafarer qualification examination is stipulated by the ministry to be held every three months. It has been held three times in Beijing and Shanghai. Now the Ministry of Communications has instructed the various Navigation Bureaus to hold the fourth qualification examination on July 27th. The location has not been specified. The Shanghai Navigation Bureau has notified all shipping companies and the Drivers' Guild after receiving the order.

Deadline for Registration 214

According to the reporter's investigation, since the Ministry of Communications implemented seafarer registration in order to issue seafarer certificates, there are still more than forty people who have not applied for certificates. Therefore, the Ministry of Communications has ordered the Navigation Bureau to instruct all seafarers to fill out resumes and apply for certificates before the end of June. If they still do not apply to the ministry by the deadline, their qualifications will be revoked and their duties suspended. The Navigation Bureau has also notified the various companies.

A Murderer at Large for Three Years Finally Caught: |Wang Lao San's Fate Escapes Not Heaven's Net| 215

Sun Jin Gen, a native of Pudong, thirty-one years old, lives in Sun Jia Zhai, Nan Jia Wan, Pudong, and makes a living selling chicks. Wang Lao San (thirty-seven years old), who used to be a plasterer, stabbed his enemy Tang Jin Long to death with a knife on April 21st, 1932. At that time, Jin Gen's father happened to be nearby. As a result, the murderer Wang Lao San escaped, and Sun's father was arrested on the spot by the police and is currently detained in the Suzhou High Court Prison. Afterwards, Sun, seeing that his father was implicated by Wang, tried his best to investigate Wang Lao San's whereabouts, hoping to bring the case to justice and exonerate his father. However, after three years, there was no trace. Unexpectedly, yesterday afternoon around 4:45, Sun went to Tang Jia Wan for business and suddenly met Wang Lao San on the way. Sun urgently called the police on duty to arrest Wang and detain him in the Second District Headquarters. After a brief interrogation by District Chief Li, the case was identified as involving a murderer, and documents were immediately prepared at 6:00 and sent to the Judicial Section for review.

Central Bank Inspection Report No. 197 219

The Central Bank's 197th Inspection Report on Issuance Reserves states: "This association is responsible for inspecting the Central Bank's issuance of convertible bond reserves in accordance with Article 15 of the Central Bank Regulations. The 197th inspection was held on May 19, 1934, at the bank's issuance bureau. The inspection results are hereby announced as follows: (A) The total amount of convertible bonds issued is 69,539,495 silver dollars, including 63,048,879 silver dollar bonds and 6,490,616 auxiliary currency bonds. The total amount of convertible bond reserves is 69,539,495 silver dollars, including 56,513,495 silver dollars in cash reserves. This cash reserve is accounted for by 53,111,684 silver dollars stored in the bank's issuance vault, 1,636,821 silver dollars stored in branch banks in various ports, 1,764,990 silver dollars stored in peer banks, and 13,026,000 silver dollars in security reserves converted into silver dollars. (B) The total amount of customs gold convertible bonds issued is 373,324.70 yuan. The total amount of customs gold convertible bond reserves is 373,324.70 yuan. This reserve includes 7,351.95 taels of standard gold, which, at a fixed price of 5.0779, is equivalent to 373,324.70 yuan in customs gold. According to Article 2 of the Central Bank's Convertible Bond Regulations, cash reserves should be 60% and security reserves should be 40%. The results of this inspection show that the cash reserve exceeds 60% and the security reserve is less than 40%, which is consistent with the regulations. This report is hereby submitted. May 21, 1934, Chairman of the Supervisory Committee of the Central Bank, Li Fu Sun, Supervisors Xie Ming Xun, Ye Song Sun, Qin Run Qing, Yu Qia Qing, Lin Kang Hou, Xu Ji Qing."

In terms of illustrations, there are color caricatures and decorative paintings by Ye Qianyu, Huang Wennong, Zhang Zhenyu, Zhang Guangyu, and Lu Shaofei, as well as photographs by Dan Duyu, Liu Xucang, Zong Weigeng, Wang Yuhuai, and many other extremely rare pictures. In terms of text, there are creative essays by Mu Shiying, Liu Na'ou, Shi Zhicun, Shao Xunmei, Ye Lingfeng, and Gao Ming, as well as introductions to works by famous French and Japanese writers. The layout format is extremely novel and breaks the existing records of domestic publications. The magazine is praised for its luxurious printing and rich content, making it a picture magazine of the highest standard, truly worthy of its name. The price is 50 cents per copy, and it is sold in various art stores. Art and literature lovers may wish to read it.

Reader's Message No. 10

Edited by the Reading Guidance Department of the Shenbao Circulation Library 226

Table of Contents (1) A Short Foreword

(2) This Week's News

(3) Special Broadcast

(A Short Foreword) Recently, many readers have often inquired about questions outside the scope of the department's work in their letters or conversations, such as, What is the future of China? What should I do? What about so-and-so important person? etc. These questions have all exceeded the scope of the department's discussion. According to the department's regulations, we could have chosen not to answer them. But whenever we encounter such questions, we cannot help but add some explanations so that readers who sincerely observe practical problems will not suspect that our attitude is insincere, or even think that we are avoiding something. But this is already quite troublesome. Now, in order to eliminate the barriers between readers, we have to declare to readers.

We have repeatedly told readers about the scope and attitude of our work. We shake hands with readers with an extremely sincere and objective attitude, standing on the position of studying learning. Whether it is a shop assistant, an apprentice, or anyone who is determined to read, we welcome them all; whatever the question, whether it is in books or closely related to books, we are willing to discuss it. To say that, of course, is not to guide readers to become bookworms, as a reader said, we are doing a bookworm-making movement. We also constantly remind readers how to combine theory and practice, but what we can do can only be limited to this. Why? First, because we believe that a person who has a foundation of social knowledge and is very concerned about the current society will not fail to understand how to deal with themselves and how to serve society. May I ask, is there anyone who is obsessed with getting promoted and making a fortune who does not know how to find money? We can fulfill our due responsibilities in the study of theory, and how to participate in practice is entirely determined by the reader themselves. We do not need to instruct, nor should we subjectively instruct. What pains us the most is that secular people are accustomed to using young people to walk their own roads, which is unfair. We are willing to be scientists, instructing some scientific truths. We are unwilling to be religious people to preach our own gospel. Second, whether it is a thing or a person, they are constantly changing and developing, and we must not evaluate them mechanically. People who were praised as loyal ministers in the past are now regarded as traitors. Therefore, for a certain thing or a certain person, we should objectively understand their growth and collapse from their own changes and from their specific manifestations. Moreover, we cannot regard a certain person or a certain thing as existing independently, but as a link in the entire social system. To subjectively and mechanically say that a certain person is good and a certain thing is bad is the most boring and inappropriate thing. Third, we ourselves are just a few people who like to read books every day, and we have no confidence that we are guides for any questions of young people, so we cannot, nor do we need to force the necessity of answering questions that we have not prepared for. Although this will inevitably disappoint some sincere readers, we are confident that we will treat people with loyalty and have a clear conscience. In terms of studying learning, we will definitely do our best to clarify any questions that we can answer. This is how it was in the past, and it will be so in the future. We hope that readers will not have too high expectations of us, nor should they be discouraged by this. We believe that our current attitude, standing in the position of an educator, is the most fair.

In the future, questions that exceed the scope of the department's work will not be answered, whether in writing or in person. We hope that everyone will have a calm mind to study theory and a pair of calm eyes to clearly observe reality.

(This Week's News) (1) How to Self-Study Social Science was delayed due to printing and only met with readers today, which is very regrettable. The original estimated price of the book was about 15 cents, but after typesetting, the number of words increased to more than 30,000, and 15 cents was not enough to cover the printing and distribution costs. There was no way but to change the price to 20 cents. We hope readers will understand. Only 1,500 copies were printed in the first edition, so buyers must buy them quickly. The general sales offices are the special distribution department of this newspaper and major bookstores in this city.

(2) The department's application form and survey form were originally two sheets, but they have now been changed to one sheet for convenience. Readers should pay attention.

(3) Readers in this city who participate in the department's procedures should first join the library to borrow books and obtain a book borrowing registration certificate before submitting an application to the department for registration.

(4) When readers in other ports who have obtained permission from the department to borrow books by mail, the department will notify the library's mail borrowing department, which will be responsible for notifying them. The department will not collect, forward, or answer questions.

(Special Broadcast) Joint Announcement of the Library Reading Club and the Youth Association 227

The reading club planned by the library has now been approved by a large number of readers, and the number of letters and applications to the library has been increasing daily. Because the library feels that the address is too small and there is no place for gatherings of more than 100 people, it has been looking everywhere for a meeting place, but it has been unable to find one. It has recently learned that the Intellectual Education Department of the Shanghai Youth Association is also preparing to open a reading club, and the association's purpose, which focuses on freedom of thought and openness of academia, is completely in line with the library's planned undertaking. Therefore, it has been agreed by both parties to merge the operations. The library's Reading Guidance Department will still send people to provide guidance on reading matters and achieve effective cooperation with the Youth Association. There will be no change in the purpose of reading. However, the Youth Association will be responsible for organizational matters in the future. The first general meeting can be convened no later than the middle of next month. The library's Reading Guidance Department will issue another notice at that time. Shenbao Circulation Library

Weather Report 228

The Zikawei Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated: Northeast China and Shandong will be sunny and hot. The wind will come from southwest to northwest, fluctuating. The lower reaches of the Yangtze River and the area around here will be sunny and hot, gradually becoming cloudy, with a southeast wind. There will be fog or misty rain in the East China Sea. The wind will be unstable and quite strong, due to a low pressure area east of Taiwan. Also, within 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 83.3 and the lowest was 61.3. On the same day last year, the highest temperature was 73.2 and the lowest was 56.8.

Sports News

Far Eastern Athletic Association Unexpectedly Illegally Dissolved by Japan and the Philippines, Another So-Called East Asian Amateur Athletic Association Formed, and the Invitation of Pseudo-Organizations Was Actually Approved, The Philippines' Flattering Japan is Lamentable 229

(Central News Agency, Manila, 21st) Because the resolutions of the 20th conference completely failed to achieve its goals, Japan forced the Philippines to reconvene at 11:00 AM on the 21st. Our country believed that the statutory two-day meeting period had passed, and the Japanese and the Philippines had greatly pressured us during the 20th meeting, so there was no need to attend again. Moreover, we did not receive the temporary notice from the Philippines on the morning of the 21st, so our representatives did not attend. In addition to the original representatives, the Japanese consul also participated in the illegally held round table meeting. The Japanese side exerted strong pressure and proposed to dissolve the Far Eastern Athletic Association and form a new association. In order to flatter Japan, the Philippines also expressed its agreement. As a result, the Far Eastern Games, which had a history of more than 20 years, was illegally terminated by the minority opinions of Japan and the Philippines. What Japan and the Philippines decided was to form another East Asian Amateur Athletic Association A m a t e u r A t h l e t i c A s s o – c i a t i o n o f T h e O r i e n t, to hold a meeting in Japan at the end of next year to discuss holding the first conference in Japan in 1938 and the second conference in the Philippines in 1940, and to invite the Dutch East Indies, Annam, India, Malaya and other countries to participate. The Philippines still stated that, under the principle of not discussing pseudo-organizations, it hopes that China will join the new association. But our country has decided to ignore this groveling and untrustworthy ugly attitude.

Ultimately Passed with Pseudo-Organization Participation 230

(Manila, 21st Dispatch) The Philippine and Japanese representatives convened today and passed a resolution to disband the Far Eastern Games and reorganize it into the East Asia Amateur Athletic Association. They immediately voted to approve the participation of pseudo-organizations. Today's meeting of Japanese and Philippine representatives swiftly passed the previously agreed-upon proposal.

The Far Eastern Athletic Association has been dissolved and the East Asia Amateur Athletic Association has been immediately established. Its organizational charter is exactly the same as the Far Eastern Association, except for Article 3 regarding membership qualifications, which only requires a two-thirds majority for approval.

The meeting also approved invitations to China and pseudo-organizations to participate. Regarding the participation of pseudo-organizations, it was agreed that upon a request for participation from the pseudo-organizations, they would be immediately allowed to join. The new officers were selected as follows:

Honorary President: Quezon, President of the Philippine Senate; President: Ryozo Hiranuma, Member of the Japanese House of Peers; Vice President: Vargas, President of the Philippine Amateur Athletic Association; Honorary Secretary: Takashi Sato, Secretary of the Japan Amateur Sports Association; Charter Committee: Iranan, Professor at the University of the Philippines, Abe, Secretary of the Japan Athletic Association.

(Dentsu Manila Express, 21st) At 11:00 AM today, the regular general meeting attended by commissioners from Japan and the Philippines discussed the dissolution of the Far Eastern Athletic Association (F.E.A.A.). The Japanese side strongly advocated for dissolution due to the current situation, and the Philippine commissioners readily agreed. Thus, Japan and the Philippines reached a consensus on the following two points: (1) Dissolve the Far Eastern Athletic Association (F.E.A.A.) and reorganize a new Oriental Amateur Athletic Association (Amateur Athletic Association of Orient). (2) The constitution of the new association will adopt the constitution of the Far Eastern Athletic Association, with only Article 3 amended to state that (the participation of new member states requires a two-thirds majority vote of the general meeting to decide). Japan and the Philippines have agreed to invite China and other Far Eastern countries, including the pseudo-state. Next, the meeting discussed the pseudo-state's participation in the Far Eastern Association. Although the Philippines had no objection to the pseudo-state's participation, given that the Far Eastern Association had already been dissolved, they agreed that the pseudo-state should join the newly formed Oriental Amateur Athletic Association and decided to urge the pseudo-state to take steps to join the new organization.

Vargas' Absurd Declaration 231

(Nippon News Agency, Manila, 21st) Constitution Drafting Committee member Vargas issued the following statement regarding this matter: "Because the meeting on the 20th ended in chaos, we reconvened on the 21st and invited commissioners from China, Japan, and the Philippines to attend. However, the Chinese representative refused to attend. We have now agreed to Japan's proposal to abolish the Far Eastern Athletic Association, and with the joint assistance of Japan and the Philippines, we are determined to invite all other countries to establish a new Oriental Athletic Association."

(Dentsu, Manila, 21st) Chairman Vargas issued a historical declaration of dissolution at today's general meeting, which decided to dissolve the assembly. The gist of the declaration was that the Chinese side should not be formally invited to attend future meetings, considering that they would not attend at any time. No other participating country has taken this attitude. Therefore, it is believed that the Far Eastern Games have been dissolved, and Japan's dissolution proposal is acknowledged. Thus, the Far Eastern Games have come to an end at its tenth session.

Illegal Revision of the Far Eastern Games Charter by Japan and the Philippines - Declaration by the Chinese Delegation 232

The Foundation of Democracy Has Been Destroyed

The Chinese Delegation is Unwilling to Be Coerced

(China News Agency, Manila, 20th) During the Far Eastern Athletic Association Congress meeting on the 20th, Japan proposed amending Article 3 of the charter. After our resolute opposition, the Philippines aided the evildoer, colluding with Japan and arbitrarily changing Article 10 to allow non-member countries to join the competition. Our representatives angrily left the venue and issued the following declaration.

Declaration by the Chinese Delegation 233

The Far Eastern Athletic Association was established twenty-one years ago with the aim of promoting international goodwill among Far Eastern countries through sports. For twenty-one years, all member countries have maintained the most cordial friendship. Now, Japan is attempting to change the charter so that any new member can join without the consent of all members. The Chinese delegation feels deeply uneasy about this. If this action is carried out, it will inevitably lead to ill feelings among member countries, which is contrary to the purpose of the association. Therefore, this delegation insists that the provisions of Article 3 of the charter should be maintained, and the admission of any new member must be approved by all members. Furthermore, this delegation also finds it difficult to recognize any other modifications to the charter aimed at circumventing the basic principles stipulated in Article 3. This delegation believes that if the procedures of today's meeting are tacitly approved without objection, the fundamental principles of democracy will be destroyed. Article 14 of the charter stipulates that amendments to the charter can be made in two ways: firstly, by a two-thirds vote of the representatives of the general meeting, and secondly, by a unanimous vote of the executive committee. There is no question about the interpretation of the latter, but opinions differ on the former. This delegation believes that the so-called representatives of the general meeting refer to a two-thirds vote of all member countries, not just the representatives attending the meeting. Otherwise, amendments to the charter can be implemented with the vote of only a few members, and any two of the five member countries can agree in advance before the meeting, persuade or coerce a third country to attend, and then amend any article of the charter. The Chinese delegation absolutely refuses to be persuaded or coerced in this way, because the charter of the general meeting is the basic law of the assembly, and any modification is of great importance, even affecting the basic rights of member countries or the existence of the assembly itself. Therefore, the Chinese delegation confirms that amendments or additions to the charter should be made with great caution, with the greatest possible consensus of all member countries, rather than being passed by a minority of member countries. Therefore, Shen Siliang stated at today's meeting that if the chairman insists on forcing the amendment of the charter to a vote, China will have no choice but to withdraw from the venue to protest this illegal action. Now that the chairman intends to put the proposal to amend the charter to a vote, and the Chinese representative has already stated everything and left the meeting, the Chinese representative is already absent. This Chinese delegation considers that any subsequent amendment of the charter is not in accordance with the regulations and makes this special declaration in the hope of public awareness. Wang Zhengting.

Shortly after, Mr. Vargas returned and the Philippine side suggested that instead of only amending the charter, it would be better to dissolve the Far Eastern Games and then reconvene around 11:00 AM. This was decided, and the entire meeting adjourned.

(Nippon News Agency, Manila, 21st) At the meeting of the New Oriental Athletic Association Establishment Committee, Mr. Abe, the Japanese representative, finally called out the names of the new officers, and the entire venue cheered to express their approval. Next, Mr. Abe expressed his opinion, stating that the dissolution of the old Far Eastern Games and the establishment of the new association and the names of its officers should be communicated to the International Olympic Committee. After the discussion, Mr. Vargas declared that the establishment of the new association was a great success and that we should look forward to its future development. Mr. Hiranuma then stated that he was very grateful for the Philippines' acceptance of Japan's wishes. The meeting adjourned at 12:40 PM.

Our Representative's Withdrawal from the Meeting Was Very Proper - So-and-So's Conversation 235

Definitive Conclusion on the Far Eastern Athletic Association 241

The 10th Far Eastern Athletic Association Games have closed. During the last two days, the Japanese representatives openly proposed to amend the charter at the annual executive committee meeting in order to promote the participation of the pseudo-state. The general meeting decided that each of the three countries would send one representative to form a special committee to discuss it. We thought this was just a customary procedure of the meeting to gloss over the matter. Who knew that something extraordinary would happen? At the second meeting, the Philippine representative, whose attitude was critical to the survival of the Far Eastern Athletic Association, suddenly changed his neutral attitude at the round table meeting held in Shanghai and openly sided with the Japanese side, plotting to illegally amend the charter. Our country's representatives, motivated by righteous indignation, withdrew from the meeting midway, while the Japanese and Philippine representatives changed their tune, arbitrarily disbanding the Far Eastern Athletic Association, completely disregarding our country, which had always tried to safeguard the Far Eastern Games, and establishing the so-called East Asia Amateur Athletic Association. What is the reason? It goes without saying that it has another purpose.

Before the 10th Far Eastern Games, the Japanese Athletic Association, in order to forcibly bring in the pseudo-organization created by its imperialism, sent a special envoy to the Philippines to lobby, and then proposed to convene a round table meeting of China, the Philippines, and Japan in Shanghai to discuss it. At that time, the reason why the Philippine representative, Dr. Tan, strictly maintained neutrality, resulting in a stalemate at the meeting, was to safeguard our country's position and dignity. The reason why the Philippine representative's attitude suddenly changed at the annual meeting was a predetermined step.

Japan proposed that the clause in Article 3 of the charter stating that the admission of new member countries must be approved by all old member countries be changed to a majority vote. Our country naturally firmly opposed it, and the Philippine representative also pretended to be affectionate, sympathizing with our country. However, it is not known that it also sympathizes with Japan on the one hand, and that non-member countries can also participate in championship competitions. Since the Philippines sympathizes with Japan on the amendment of this article of the charter, it is clear that Article 3 of the charter is no longer effective. In this way, even if the pseudo-organization does not join the Far Eastern Athletic Association as a formal member, it can participate in official competitions. Furthermore, judging from the current political situation in the Far East and the relationship after the Philippines declared independence, the attitude of the Philippine representatives this time was absolutely instructed by another background, so they did not hesitate to take this decisive measure. It is also very obvious.

Although the Far Eastern Games have a history of twenty years, there are no clear regulations in the organization, relying entirely on the gentlemanly spirit of sports as the only creed. It was not until the 9th Far Eastern Games held in Tokyo in May 1930 that the existing official charter was established. The reason was that there was once an atmosphere in 1929 for Goryeo to request to join, and in order to prevent Goryeo from joining, Japan not only had to specify the charter, but also paid special attention to the fact that the admission of new member countries must be approved by all old member countries. Now that it is impossible for Goryeo to join, unexpectedly, the pseudo-organization has risen, and Japan has disregarded everything again, plotting to overthrow the provisions it previously proposed to establish, thus forming today's great waves in the Far Eastern Athletic Association. It belongs to one person to renege, and its sinister means and despicable intentions are obvious.

Furthermore, the Dutch East Indies and Vietnam have officially joined as members. Even if the charter is amended, it only needs to be passed by a majority of members, but the representatives of the Dutch East Indies and Vietnam did not attend and declared their abstention. Since our country has opposed it, even though Japan and the Philippines have agreed, it is only two countries. This is completely inconsistent with public reason and the spirit of amending the charter. It is an oppression of the majority by the minority. After our country's representatives withdrew in righteous indignation, the Japanese and Philippine representatives disregarded the spirit of harmony and concerted efforts in the past ten years and resolutely plotted to dissolve the Far Eastern Athletic Association, illegally organizing the so-called East Asia Amateur Athletic Association, rejecting our country, the originator of the Far Eastern Games, far away, and inviting our country and the pseudo-state to participate with an objective attitude. If this is tolerable, what is not tolerable? In short, Japan is the executioner who destroyed the Far Eastern Athletic Association, and the Philippines is its executioner. Where is the spirit? Where is public reason? Since Japan and the Philippines do not hesitate to destroy the Far Eastern Games, which have been vigorously maintained for 20 years with harmony and concerted efforts, why should our country continue to believe in the creed of sportsmanship? It is time to withdraw resolutely.

The New Authority in Our Country's Tennis Circles - The Course of the China Tennis Club's Initiative - Gather Tennis Stars from Our Country to Train Young Athletes - Build the Finest Tennis Courts in the Far East with Tens of Thousands of Dollars - Members Include Lin Baohua, Xu Chengji, Qiu Feihai, etc. 242

Tan Jingjun, the general manager of Huaye Trust Company, has always had enthusiasm for sports, especially tennis. In view of the depression in the Shanghai tennis circle and the control of our country's players by Westerners, Wan Shan, tennis giants Lin Baohua, Qiu Feihai, Xu Chengji, Zheng Zhaojia, and other enthusiasts, launched the large-scale China Tennis Club, Cathay Tenois Club. The location was chosen on Singapore Road (near the intersection of Connaught Road and Little Xiasaw Road). Mr. Tan donated 14 acres of private property and invested 30,000 yuan to build the site and arrange everything. It is now ready. Details are as follows:

Purpose of Initiation 243

Throughout history, the authority of tennis in Shanghai has been controlled by Westerners, and the Shanghai Chinese Tennis Club, affiliated to the National Sports Association, has always been lifeless. In addition, the site is about to be recovered, and famous players are not enough to improve their skills, and young talents are also buried, and they are not enough to improve their technology. In view of this, this large-scale tennis club was launched. In the future, it is planned to launch more official competitions, invite famous foreign players to perform in Shanghai, and send our country's players to compete abroad, etc., to promote young players and aim to revitalize tennis in our country. The exquisite architecture of the tennis court is especially a model for the Far East.

Break Away from Westerners 244

The joint competition of the Shanghai Westerner Lawn Tennis Club will start on the 30th of this month. The Chinese team, the champion of the previous session, has already joined, but the person in charge of the club, in view of the fact that China's first-class players such as Lin, Qiu, Xu, Zheng, and Yu are all in it, actually excluded the participation of the Chinese team due to the strength of our team. Lin Baohua was very angry, so they unanimously and resolutely decided not to cooperate with the lawn tennis club and would not participate in any competitions of the lawn tennis club. In this way, the ticket revenue of the lawn tennis club will be cut off, and the economy will inevitably panic. The Chinese Tennis Club will independently host all competitions in Shanghai and invite four people to join the competitions hosted by our Chinese people in order to fight for the dignity of the tennis circle in our country.

Tennis Court Architecture 245

The tennis courts and houses are designed and built by architect Li Jinpei and carefully arranged by Tan Shuping. Four ordinary tennis courts are temporarily set up for ordinary practice. Two special tennis courts are built for competition. The construction of these special tennis courts is completely modeled after the structure of the Wimbledon Central Court in England. The two courts cost more than 10,000 yuan. This kind of tennis court is the first of its kind in the Far East. Wooden stands are built around it, which can accommodate three to four thousand spectators. They are gradually being completed. The cost has reached 30,000 yuan. In the future, it is planned to build a model clubhouse at a cost of 80,000 yuan in order to achieve perfection.

Membership Fees 246

In addition to promoting tennis, the club also plans to cover the tennis courts with canopies in winter to hold badminton competitions. Many of our country's tennis players are famous in this field. After the tennis courts and other arrangements are completed, an executive committee must be elected to strictly organize. Lin Baohua has been appointed as the secretary to preside over everything. After Xu Chengji returns to Shanghai from Manila this time, he will stay in Shanghai and will not go to Java anymore. He and Qiu Feihai are both basic members of the club. The annual membership fee for the tennis section is 50 yuan, 35 yuan for women, and 30 yuan for the badminton section. If you join both the tennis and badminton sections at the same time, the annual membership fee is 70 yuan. There are already 70 to 80 members. The future development is limitless. It is a good phenomenon in our country's tennis circle.

Hua Zhong Games Closed 247

(Central News Agency, Hankou, 21st) The Hua Zhong Games ended. The closing ceremony was held on the 11th morning. About 600 people attended, including Cheng Qibao, Zhang Qun, and the officials and athletes of the conference. Chairman Cheng Qibao also delivered a speech, saying that the conference was held for six days and everything was smooth. The results of various events were almost on par with national records. Although there were minor twists and turns, they were resolved satisfactorily by all parties, which was a good phenomenon. Zhang Qun then delivered a speech, still encouraging the spirit of unity of the four provinces, and encouraging the athletes to work hard to train and establish merits in the Far Eastern Games. Liu Minggao, Wu Guozhen, and others then spoke. Finally, the representative of Hunan, Fang Kegang, gave a reply. Chief Referee Cheng Dengke reported the results, and Yu Fengzhi and others gave awards. The ceremony ended at 11:00 AM. It is reported that the athletes from various provinces will soon leave Hankou and return to their provinces.
