Page 14

Comprehensive Review of the 10th Far East Games, Inscribed by Wu Tiecheng

Review and Prospect by Pan Gongzhan 262

Only with a healthy citizenry can there be a healthy nation. Physical education is part of education, used to train the citizens and give them healthy bodies. Education without physical education is like building a tall building on sand. Sports meets are one way to check on the physical education of the citizens. In addition to winning and losing, sports meet also cultivates the spirit of cooperation and unity, the courage to struggle, and advances them on the road to vitality and strength. Thus, in the National Games, we can see how advanced the physical education of the provinces and cities are. In the International Games, we can see how advanced the physical education of the various nations are. This is why the Far East Games are worthy of our attention.

Various causes in our country have yet to fully get on track, and physical education has been affected as well. The Far East Games have gone on for ten sessions to this point, and yet our country's performance in the Far East Games has declined more and more with each passing year, to the point where we are not competitive at all. Although one might say that winning and losing is unrelated to the spirit of physical education, the fact that our skills are far inferior to others is, after all, an undeniable fact. If our skills do not improve, then the advancement of our physical education will also be delayed. Thus, those who are assessing the sports meet should also assess the skills, in addition to the winning and losing.

Today, the tenth Far East Games in Manila, Philippines, have concluded after ten days of competition. How our country has fared, and how our skills have advanced and declined are things that we must review and inspect in order to understand the evolution of their country's physical education cause, as well as to use it as our own reference. Then we will no longer linger without advancing, and the health of the citizenry will also trend towards strength day by day. This is what all the gentlemen who are writing these assessments all hope for.

Moreover, I am particularly aware that before the opening of this Far East Games, the Japanese representatives presumptuously hoped to invite the puppet state of Manchukuo to participate, resulting in a foul atmosphere. Fortunately, the Philippines understood the big picture, and the games were able to take place. Unexpectedly, before the closing of the games, the Philippines actually disregarded justice and colluded with Japan to privately amend the charter, hoping that the puppet state of Manchukuo could participate in the next games. It is truly unknown what their intention is. Our country's representatives, argued on the basis of reason and withdrew from the meeting as a whole, and their attitude was very proper. But from this, we deeply feel the weakness of our national power, and that we are insulted everywhere. Only after suffering bitter lessons will the whole nation, from top to bottom, be vigilant day and night in order to seek self-improvement. Thus, the strengthening of our national physique is something we should not neglect even more.

Now, Shanghai China-America Tobacco Company, acting on this intention, has issued a special publication assessing the Far East Games. In addition to promoting domestic goods, they are also paying attention to the accomplishments of our nation's physical education. Their spirit is truly admirable. I secretly hope that my colleagues in the education and physical education circles can encourage each other, so that the actions of the China-America Tobacco Company will not have been in vain. Thus, I will use a few words to begin.

Track and Field By a Reporter from Shishi Daily 263

— Teng Shugu

The track and field championships of this Far East Games have both been won by Japan. They set five new records in track events, and two new records in field events. The Philippines is also not weak. The most miserable thing is that our country still came away with zero points in the track events. Even Liu Changchun and others did not make a name for themselves in the preliminaries. The field events were a bit more comforting, and scored six points more than in the previous session. Thus, Wu Bixian's fourth place in the high jump, and Chen Baoqiu's second place in the shot put and Fu Baolu's second place in the pole vault have become topics of conversation.

However, this absolutely cannot be taken as optimism or satisfaction. It must be understood that our progress is still as slow as an oxcart. Compared to other countries, the difference cannot be measured in distance. We should know where our problems lie, and why other countries are advancing so rapidly. In short, it is due to the poor economic conditions in all respects (including politics, education, economics, and society), such as how Begali won first place in the 1500 meters at the Olympics, and how fascist countries have "flying legs", all because of Mussolini's encouragement. To put it feudally, Yue Fei used his spear to defeat the young Liang Wang and became the top martial arts scholar, and there is a reason for that (this saying is still extremely implicit).

(1) Education is not universal, schools lack forced exercise, and many are just going through the motions. Most athletes did not receive basic training in elementary school, show off in middle school, and play around in university when they feel like it. After graduation (closing time, everything is over.)

(2) Athletes' lives are unstable. Many take the path of physical education teachers. When their achievements are significant, they show off and become teachers, losing their amateur status.

(3) How many athletic fields are there in major and minor schools and towns across the country where people can feel the urge to play spontaneously? (The importance of athletic fields can be seen from the story of "Athletic King" Pasqueden).

(4) There is a shortage of track and field teachers who have solid experience, are very rich, and are good at teaching. Those who are boastful, do nothing in their position, and mislead students are everywhere.

(5) There is a lack of competition opportunities. If there are any, they are just annual sports meetings. They are just advertisements for the school.

(6) We rarely send people to the world track and field stage to observe, nor do we invite advanced track and field athletes from other countries to perform in China. How can we get on the right track if we build cars behind closed doors?

(7) Most track and field athletes have no restraint in their diet and daily life.

(8) They do not know how to specialize. Track and field athletes are almost all-rounders. They want to play basketball, soccer, and everything else. In order to win glory for the school, they do everything from 100 meters to 800 meters. They rarely practice regularly and often sharpen their spears before the battle. How can they get good results? (9) The social atmosphere is too bad, there are too many bad habits, and people do not pay attention to track and field. They scold the losers and blindly praise the winners, while the critics are people who do not participate in sports at all.

The complaints are not finished yet, and it is already late. Let's stop here.

Soccer By a Reporter from Shen Bao 264

— Shen Zhenchao

The Far East Games soccer championship is our country's traditional possession, and every session has been ours. Other countries have the intention to get involved, but lack the ability. Unexpectedly, in the battle in Tokyo in the previous session, Japan rose up and tied our country 3-3. They did not dare to have a final match with us, so the championship was split between China and Japan, which was a great regret. In this Far East Games, our country's soccer team had great determination to wash away this shame. Sure enough, news came that they won all three matches, defeating the Philippines, then defeating the Dutch East Indies, and finally defeating Japan, maintaining the prestige of our ever-victorious army. The thing we wanted most in this session was this championship, so its value cannot be overstated.

Pre-Match Situation Before the match, although we had the determination to win the championship, we were worried, given the poor results of the previous session, that we would repeat the same mistakes. The Philippines knew that their strength was not to be feared, while soccer was the strength of Java, with many famous players and formidable strength. In addition to the Dutch East Indies, there was Japan. After the athletes arrived safely in the Philippines, news came that, according to the on-the-spot observation of our country's coach Huang Jiajun, the Japanese were mediocre in skills and not to be feared. Thus, the determination to win was even greater.

Jiang Bai's Contributions In the first match, a good news came, we defeated the Philippines 2-0. We failed to score in the first half, but in the second half, Tan Jiangbai scored with a header, opening the scoring. Li Huitang followed up with another goal. In the second match, we faced the famous Dutch East Indies Java team. They defeated Japan 7-1 the previous day. Facing a strong enemy, we could not act rashly. Some of our compatriots also played on their team. Unexpectedly, another good news came, we won again 2-0. Cao Guicheng scored first, followed by Tan Jiangbai. With the strong enemy defeated, the championship was secure. Sure enough, in the last match, we defeated Japan 4-3 again. Li Tiansheng was sent off, resulting in this situation. Tan Jiangbai scored two consecutive goals, making the score 2-0. Li Huitang followed, making it 4-3. Looking at the three matches as a whole, Jiangbai scored the most goals and was indeed our country's hero. The telegrams also stated that his performance was the most satisfying.

Chu Talents Use Talents Although the championship has been won by us, the most regrettable and lamentable thing is that there were five compatriots on the Dutch East Indies team. It is a truly sad thing that they cannot serve their motherland. Their soccer skills are all outstanding, and they have stated that they are happy to serve if the motherland needs them. Therefore, we hope that our country's authorities will pay attention to the talents among the overseas compatriots when selecting representatives next time. In terms of strength, the Dutch East Indies are the strongest after our country. Although they lost to the Philippines later, the score was 2-3, but the Dutch East Indies were leading 2-1 in the first half. Other situations may have caused the situation to change suddenly.

Rough Actions The Philippines lost to Japan 3-4 and defeated the Dutch East Indies 3-2. The runner-up was a triangular situation. The Philippines were the home team, and they had all the advantages of time and place. It is a pity that their actions were rough, barbaric, and frightening, resulting in six or seven of our team members being injured in the first match between China and the Philippines. Looking at the soccer situation in the previous Far East Games, the actions of the Philippines may also be a hereditary habit. Is this so?

Endurance Wins The Japanese lost to the Dutch East Indies 1-7, but were able to defeat the Philippines 4-3 and fought hard with us 3-4. Their only advantage is their endurance. Endurance is one of the most important factors in winning a competition. Success or failure all depend on the final effort. Although the Japanese were defeated by us, this is something we should emulate. In their match against the Philippines, they were behind 1-3 in the first half, but were able to score three consecutive goals in the second half and turn defeat into victory. In the match against us, when they were behind 1-3, they were able to tie the score at 3-3. Although the circumstances were different, their continuous and unrelenting spirit of struggle is where their success lies in all their causes. We should learn from this.

Unlimited Hope Now that we have won this championship, and washed away the previous shame, time flies like an arrow, and waits for no one. There is also the World Games and the next Far East Games. Although there is still time, it will be here in the blink of an eye. We cannot be negligent because there are still many thorns in the road ahead. We hope that the athletes who win glory for the country and return in triumph will continue to work hard and tirelessly. The future is full of hope.

All-Around Times Reporter 265

— Zhang Shengzhi

When the all-around athletic events began, the games were already nearing their end. This competition was only between Japan and the Philippines. Our country sent Wang Jihai, Zhang Lingjia, and Liu Renxiu to participate in the pentathlon and decathlon. Failure was expected. However, the efforts of Wang, Zhang, and Liu were deeply appreciated by all parties, their spirit commendable, and their performance passable.

In the pentathlon, the Japanese army displayed its prowess, with the Philippine army following closely behind. Although our Wang Jihai worked hard for the country from beginning to end, his strength was limited, and he ultimately failed to achieve his desires. Therefore, this competition was like a solo stage for the Japanese, dominating the entire field and monopolizing the top four spots.

In the decathlon, the Philippines' Meyers was truly strong and skilled. It was predicted beforehand that he would win the championship. In the first half, Meyers immediately took the lead with 3698.54 points. Our Liu Renxiu was eliminated. Zhang Lingjia also occupied sixth place with 3250.65 points. In addition, Japan's Murakami, Asakuma Yoshiro, Ogura Keiji, and the Philippines' Ponsel occupied the second, third, fourth, and fifth positions, respectively. As the second half began, Meyers continued to look down upon everything and moved forward, while the others fell behind and were eliminated one after another. Jinzi Fangxiong, Qi Chenxiong, and A. Portugal, who were unknown in the first half, suddenly rose up and occupied very advantageous positions. Zhang Lingjia's poor performance in the pole vault and 1500 meters led to the abandonment of all his previous efforts, and he failed.

In the 1600-meter relay, the competition between Japan and the Philippines was extremely fierce. The Philippines had a clear advantage in the first three legs, leading Japan by as much as three meters. Our team lagged far behind due to insufficient strength. The final leg featured an extremely fierce competition. Japan's Masuda managed to catch up to Aranbrey. At the finish line, the Philippines won by the chest. The time was three minutes and thirty-three seconds, with the Japanese team at three minutes and thirty-five seconds, both setting new records for the games. Compared to them, we have feelings that are unbearable to look back on. However, it is hoped that the athletes will continue to work hard after returning to their country. The future is still within reach. Encourage them, and warn them.

The 400-meter relay can be said to be Japan's revenge battle. From beginning to end, the two sides seemed to be on the same level, with no clear distinction between them. In the end, Japan narrowly defeated the Philippine army. Our country's crushing defeat goes without saying. The time was 42.3 seconds, while the Philippines obtained 42.4 seconds. The tension of the battle can be seen from the above results.

Swimming Morning News Reporter 266

— Qu Yue

Swimming is vigorously promoted by all countries in the world, and progress is made every year. Our country is still in its infancy in this area. Except for some talent in the coastal provinces, almost no one promotes it in the interior. It is really difficult to catch up with other countries. The reasons for this are: first, insufficient promotion; second, a lack of coaching talent; third, a lack of swimming pool construction; and fourth, a failure to conduct in-depth research on methods. With these four points, an uneven situation is formed, with distorted development and slow progress. This is an undeniable fact.

In the swimming championships of the Far Eastern Games, our country only won in the second session. All other years, we have fallen behind. And afterwards, we only scored slightly in the third and fourth sessions. The rest of the time, we have not been able to open up a scoring record. Although there has been progress in recent years, compared with Japan and the Philippines, it is like a thousand miles away. Moreover, our country's victory in the second session was not due to the excellence of our country's results, but because Japan and the Philippines did not yet know the importance of this sport. As of today, Japanese athletes have made rapid progress, surpassing the Philippines by a large margin. How about our country? In the 10th World Games, Japan even overwhelmed the United States (the kingdom of water) and won the world throne. Let alone the Far East? Dominating the stage, who would say it is not appropriate?

Although it is not appropriate to magnify the spirit of others and diminish one's own prestige, how should our country promote and develop? If this continues, not only will we not be able to compete with Japan and the Philippines, but even the desire to wash away the shame of zero points is just a dream.

Philippine athlete Irtaifonso has consecutively maintained the first place in the breaststroke of the Far Eastern Games for four sessions. He is truly the most glorious athlete in the history of the Far Eastern Games. Even Japan's Tsuruta and Koike, who once dominated the world stage, were defeated by him, which is really admirable. We should know that taking the highest standard as a model is not only true for swimming.

Promote physical fitness to strengthen the country. Ma Chonggan respectfully inscribed.

Women's Swimming News Reporter 267

— Shen Meizhen

From our country's perspective, the most praiseworthy aspect of this Far Eastern Games is the women's swimming exhibition match. Our representative, the mermaid Yang Xiuqiong, shook the Philippines, winning three championships and winning the individual title with fifteen points. Other ladies also had good performances, almost monopolizing all the awards. This is truly one of the most glorious pages for our country in the Far Eastern Games. Our delegation has a total of four people: Yang Xiuqiong, Liu Guizhen, Chen Huanqiong, and Liang Yongxian. They are all Hong Kong female athletes who shined in last year's National Games. These four can almost be regarded as the four outstanding women swimmers in our country. Women's swimming started at 5 pm on the fifth day of the games (that is, the 16th), at the same time as men's swimming. The first day's events included the 50-meter freestyle, 200-meter breaststroke, and 200-meter relay. Japan did not participate, and only China and the Philippines competed. Our four representatives initially showed their skills and immediately made a splash. We won all three championships. Yang Xiuqiong set an excellent record of 36.93 seconds in the 50-meter freestyle. Liu Guizhen also got third, with a score of 38 seconds. Both broke the national record. The second and fourth places were for Philippine women. Yang Xiuqiong originally belonged to the first place in the 200-meter breaststroke, with a time of 3 minutes and 41.2 seconds. Unfortunately, Ms. Yang only used one hand to touch the pool wall when turning, which caused her to be disqualified. Chen Huanqiong, who was second, was promoted to first place, with a time of 3 minutes and 58.4 seconds. Liu Guizhen was second, and a Philippine woman was third. In the 200-meter relay, the competition between the two sides was extremely fierce. Liu Guizhen swam first for our side and lagged behind by one meter. Chen Huanqiong and Liang Yongxian followed and still lagged behind. Yang Xiuqiong chased hard and surpassed in the last three meters, creating a new record of 2 minutes and 41.7 seconds.

The next day, all competitions were stopped due to rain. They continued on the 18th. Yang Xiuqiong won two more first places. She created a time of 1 minute and 27.5 seconds in the 100-meter freestyle, overwhelming the three Philippine women. She shortened the 100-meter backstroke to 1 minute and 38 seconds. Liang Yongxian also won third place. In summary, except for the 200-meter breaststroke, the other four events broke our country's highest record. It can be seen that the progress of each person is truly commendable. In the swimming pool, because our representative repeatedly won, our national flag was raised repeatedly, and the national anthem was played repeatedly. The audience applauded non-stop, and they obtained supreme glory. When our representatives first arrived in the Philippines, the Filipinos made boring criticisms, saying that our representatives came to compete for beauty. At this point, the Filipinos began to look at each other in shock and praised them as "Miss China." Women's swimming will be changed to a championship event in the next session. It has been decided at the Swimming Committee meeting on the 18th, but it still needs to be submitted to the Executive Committee of the Far Eastern Games for discussion. It will most likely become a reality. Then our female athletes must continue to work hard, prepare for the next competition, maintain the existing hegemony, and the honor of the country will also be involved.

Spring and Autumn

Misty Records of Imperial Incense 275

— Originally written by Princess Der Ling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

In front of this Phoenix Carriage, there was a short, small door. When the Empress Dowager was boarding the carriage, Li Lianying would first open it. The Empress Dowager would then step through the opening, slowly turning around to rest her back against the soft cushion behind her, her face facing forward, comfortably seated in this box-shaped mobile room. When ordinary people rode in sedan chairs, the carriers often unintentionally made their shoulders rise and fall, causing the person inside to be jostled and uncomfortable. However, those carrying the Phoenix Carriage would never dare to behave like this.

On both sides of the Empress Dowager's seat, there were armrests covered in yellow satin with silk floss, especially for her to rest her arms. Besides these armrests, right in front of her chest was that short door-like thing. There was also a narrow wooden board on it, generally covered in yellow satin, very soft and smooth. If the Empress Dowager wanted to lean forward, she could comfortably rest on this door, because its ends were fastened with iron buttons, so it would never shake.

This board, which could be leaned on, was about five or six inches wide and could be lifted up. To put it more clearly, under this board, though nominally the small door of the Phoenix Carriage, was actually a rectangular, flat box. Because it was made to be exactly the same width as the carriage, it served both purposes: a small door and a table for the Empress Dowager. The person who designed this was truly ingenious for that time! So, what was placed inside this rectangular, flat box? Of course, there were things inside! The first thing was the Empress Dowager's powder puff, and the second thing was a short jade ruler. However, this ruler was round, and the Empress Dowager often used it to rub her face, seemingly to reduce wrinkles. (39)

University Students' Worries 276

— Only Via

University students naturally have plenty of money at home. As the saying goes, "With money, you can make the devil push the millstone." So, how can a university student with the economic means still have worries?

It is said that university students also have genuine worries. The first is not winning the favor of a queen or princess. Even though one is a handsome university student, for the sake of the queen or princess, one does not hesitate to condescend and curry favor. After spending three days and three nights drafting a flawless and concrete plan to attack the queen or princess, what is the result? The queen or princess, however, shows intimacy with another classmate, arm in arm or embracing. Losing both the lady and the army, how can a university student not be worried?

Second, the exam date is approaching. The famous bookworm in the class refuses to help. The professor is stern and refuses to narrow down the scope. With all roads blocked and no solution in sight, Heaven's help is not as good as man's help, and man's help is not as good as self-help. It is best to burn the midnight oil and prepare late into the night. But after looking at the second page, one forgets the first page. After looking at the third page, one simply looks at it without understanding anything. If one fails the exam and is held back, the old man at home will be angry and cut off the economic supply, which is not something to be taken lightly. This is naturally cause for worry.

After completing the course and looking around for a while, one graduates because of the virtue accumulated by one's ancestors. At this time, one has to worry about one's future after graduation. Should one study abroad? One knows oneself and knows one's illness, fearing there is no hope. Should one seek employment? One disdains small positions, and one's abilities are not sufficient for large positions. Heavens, how worrying!

The Way to Save the Nation 277

— Maple Child

After the decline of the incense market in Hangzhou, the banks of West Lake have added a vibrant scenery since the Kalachakra initiation ceremony for the rebirth of the Panchen Lama. Some come from the sea to join the festivities, some come from Nanjing to pay their respects, and there are also local devout men and women and curious people who want to see the Tibetan living Buddha. The lonely Six Bridges and Three Temples, covered with fallen flowers, have regained the joy of spring in the flying dust.

Hearing that the Dharma assembly can promote world peace, then Buddhism can save the country. China, which is poor and weak, is far from the enemy of its strong neighbors in terms of military weapons. Instead of shouting empty slogans of armed resistance, it is better for everyone to close their doors and recite a chapter of the scriptures. Occasionally flipping through old newspapers, I saw a headline with a startling title: (The righteous act of overthrowing the puppet state failed, and the patriot Gao Chengzhang was arrested!) Needless to say, after cruel torture and interrogation, the patriot died for his country! I am reminded of Jiang Minsheng, an anti-Japanese hero, wandering on the sea and crying for food. It cannot be denied that their righteous actions, although they were willing to sacrifice their lives to save the country, cannot be severely blamed for their foolishness, but throwing eggs against stones is also not favored by the wise.

I think that although the purpose of saving the country is the same, the methods do not have to copy old articles. Everyone should do their best and take their own path. Why bother to imitate moths flying into the flame? To give an analogy: those who do business should try every means to seek profit, those who study should study their books diligently, and those who have free time may as well work hard to strengthen their bodies. And so on.

In short, success is easily achieved at the right time and in the right place (position). Otherwise, one will take a detour in vain and still be scolded as: (Fool!)

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 29: Reply Letter Reveals Heartbreak, Vowing to Live Alone; Listening Together, Swearing Loyalty with Blood

After thinking for a while, Jiang said firmly, "There's no need to read the letter. Just tell me the gist of it." Gui Zhi said, "You understand my past. Although I know Gan Erye, it's only because he's a neighbor. I have nothing else with him." Jiang said, "We don't need to talk about the past. Let's just talk about the present." If the Zhao family finds out, I naturally won't be able to live as a human being. But you'll also let people talk about why you raised such a girl." Jiang said, "Alright, stop talking. It'll be over if you ignore him in the future." Gui Zhi said, "If it would be over if I ignored him, I wouldn't be talking so much nonsense." Jiang said, "If you ignore him, what can he do?" Gui Zhi said, "I'm not ignoring you because I think he wouldn't dare to do anything. It's just that if I don't cut off his thoughts, it'll seem like I acquiesced to him writing this letter. After pondering for a long time, she asked, "According to your meaning, are you planning to write him a reply?" Gui Zhi said sternly, "Don't misunderstand things. Replying is just replying, but there are many ways to reply. For example, I can honestly say in the letter that he shouldn't do this, and if he writes again, I'll announce it. Tell me, would he still be embarrassed to write to me again if I said that? Anyway, we don't see each other, so it doesn't matter if I offend him." (389)

Lonely Snoring 279

Handball Craze 280

— Xie Jijue

Playing handball is a wonderful sport, and it's now sweeping the whole school! Perhaps it's also popular in other places?

A tennis ball, the kind used in plays, is thrown against the wall, and it bounces back. The second person has to catch it and throw it back. The performance continues in this way, and whoever can't catch it loses. The number of losses is used to compare who is better or worse. It's quite fun to play with a few people, and it's also considered a full-body workout. You use your hands, but you also have to aim with your eyes. At the same time, your feet have to run, your brain has to think, and your body has to twist and turn. So, no part of you is left unused. Moreover, this is not a sport that requires a lot of brute force, and it's especially welcomed by students who are not interested in sports.

At first, only a few people played on the outer wall of the dormitory. Gradually, everyone became interested, and more people played. As a result, one or two windowpanes on the wall had to be broken every day. As a result, the glass on the windows was reduced indefinitely. It was inconvenient to have windows without glass, and it was another loss to replace them. The dormitory manager (off-campus dormitory) was very worried, but there was no way to prohibit it. To cater to their preferences and avoid glass losses, he cleverly built a wall more than ten feet high in the open space behind the dormitory, coated it with cement, and drew red lines. This was much more suitable than an ordinary wall. As for the school, the physical education department has also commissioned the construction of a wooden sign for students who play handball.

Handball, it is said, is also a kind of ball sport. But in our school, this handball game was used by students who failed to return from the racquetball court to relieve boredom, and it gradually aroused the interest of the public. So, you often hear students saying, "Let's go play racquetball!" What is called (racquetball) here is (handball).

World Oddities

— Bingyu

Blind Female Student 281

In Radcliffe University in Massachusetts, USA, there is a blind female student named Daniel. Her personality is very strong. She often says that blind people should be respected. Recently, the university held a swimming competition, and she actually won first place. The students all avoided her, and she is also proficient in English, French, and Latin. She is especially good at history and English literature. She is now focusing on studying law and diligently practicing finger Braille, preparing to become a lawyer in the future.

Cat Appointed as French Official 282

The French lower house has officially appointed two cats as candidate officials this time. Because the French lower house is located in the Palais Bourbon in Paris, since the previous parliament, mice have suddenly multiplied, and the valuable decorations in the palace have been damaged by mice. The members of parliament believed that it was necessary to keep cats, so they selected two fierce cats and kept them in the courtyard, and also named them candidate officials.

Rare Postcard 283

A painter from Munich, Germany, named Pei Erhal, Xiuma Xier, can write 121,628 words on an ordinary postcard. That is, he wrote Hitler's book (My Struggle) on the postcard in 236 lines, but the text cannot be identified. It must be magnified with a 40x microscope to be understood. It is said that Pei spent 64 hours writing this postcard, which is also a rare record of fine writing in the world.

Error in the Calendar 284

German astronomer Si Huaer De. Gelong Haer published a surprising theory. He said that this year is 1941, not 1934. According to his investigation, 1941 years ago (7 years before the Christian era), Saturn appeared in the Pisces constellation. At that time, there was a rumor among the Jewish people that when any changes occurred in the Pisces constellation in the east, they could break away from Roman rule, and the king of all nations on earth would surely be born from the Jewish people. For example, the birth of Christ was based on astrology and divination. The discovery of this extraordinary person's birth was Saturn, so it is judged that this year is 1941.

History of Human Struggle 285

Recently, the French International Association published an article. It says that in the past 3,400 years, humans have been able to sleep peacefully for only 268 years. In the remaining 3,132 years, hundreds of millions of lives have been sacrificed in war. Although humans all yearn for lasting peace and advocate non-war, international treaties have been concluded more than 8,000 times, but after implementation, their effectiveness lasts for a maximum of two years. After two years, conflicts will occur. Therefore, the history of mankind can simply be called a history of struggle.

Female Hero of Soviet Russia 286

The female brigade commander of Soviet Russia, who also serves as the captain of the air force, Shi Maluoge Weiya, has an experience in the air. At first, she rode in an unpowered aircraft. One day, she and her cousin were riding together, and unfortunately they crashed. Her cousin broke his left leg, and the lady was also slightly injured. She originally graduated from the Lenin Red Army Aviation School, and was later assigned to the Red Army flying team. She is now the captain of the Red Army Air Force. The total flying time has reached 1,000 hours today, which is truly the leader of women in the world.

Mule Overturns Train 287

Near Walla Walla, Washington, USA, there was a mule that was grazing on the tracks of the Northern Pacific Railway. One day, a train was heading north, and the mule was still standing still. The driver on the locomotive gave a loud signal, but the mule jumped to the side of the switch and overturned the train. Nineteen passengers in the car were injured, but the mule was unharmed. This is a strange story in a report from the American Accident Insurance Company.

Silk and Tea The Weather Suddenly Warms; Spring Silkworms' Sleep Period Varies 299

(Shangyu) This year, farmers in the Linxi Township and Henghe Town areas, seeing the lush mulberry leaves, all began raising spring silkworms. However, due to the decline of the rural economy and lack of funds to purchase seeds, the number of farmers incubating local varieties is not small. This spring, due to excessive rainfall and cold weather, the development of improved varieties has been slower. Fortunately, instructors have been doing their best to provide guidance, minimizing losses. Local silkworm varieties have weaker resistance and have suffered significant damage, with many farmers replenishing with late-spring silkworms. The timing of the silkworm season varies. Recently, with clear and warm weather, silkworm larvae have been developing healthily. Early batches have already entered their major sleep, while late batches are still in their third sleep. Leaf prices are low and lack a stable market value.

(Shengxian) In the various villages in southern and northern Shengxian, this year many farmers are raising self-retained local silkworm varieties. However, due to adverse weather, six or seven out of ten of the early batches were discarded. Therefore, they are all replenishing with improved varieties, with instructors paying attention to breeding and providing full scientific protection, resulting in fewer losses. However, the timing of silkworm sleep varies. Early batches have already entered their major sleep and are spinning leaves, while late batches are just starting their third sleep. In recent days, the weather has been sunny and warm, and silkworm larvae development has been progressing smoothly.

(Baima) The Baima and Xinfeng areas of He Prefecture have always been improved silkworm areas. This year, many are raising improved varieties. Mulberry leaf prices are low, and the number of larvae has surged. However, the number of farmers raising self-retained local silkworm varieties is also not small. Silkworm sleep is uneven, with sluggish development during the first sleep. Later, fortunately, the weather turned clear, with gentle breezes and warm sunshine, and silkworm larvae development has been very good. Currently, early silkworms are already in their third sleep and spinning leaves, while late silkworms are still in their second sleep. Leaf prices are only four or five dimes per load, with no market for leaf futures.

(Haimen) In recent years, silkworm farming in various villages has been declining. This year, due to the cold weather, mulberry trees sprouted later, and the silkworm season is also late. Larval growth is weak. Improved varieties account for five or six out of ten, and larvae collection has been delayed. After the first sleep, due to continuous rain, silkworm larvae development has been unhealthy. Instructors have been working to provide assistance, minimizing losses for improved varieties. Local silkworm varieties, due to their weak resistance, have mostly been lost. Recently, with clear and warm weather, both early and late silkworms have been developing smoothly. Early batches are starting their third sleep, while late batches are spinning leaves from the second sleep. There are few silkworms and plenty of leaves, with no stable market price.

Free Talk

Scientific Spirit Medium 309

— A Proverb

Religion and scholarship are weighed against each other; religion is valued more than scholarship, and scholarship is needed more urgently than religion. In reality, this is a highly disputable issue. We moderns have neither scholarship nor religion, so we probably won't have much interest in this issue.

We have superstition but no religion, and heresy but no science. However, modern science has advanced, Eastern culture is about to revive, and foreign devils are about to be driven back, and the evidence is (scientific spirit medium).

(Spirit medium) is a Chinese national treasure, and science is a Western essence. A national treasure plus a Western essence is suitable for men and women of all ages throughout the country. Westerners see it as a Chinese product, and Chinese see it as a Western product, satisfying both the psychology of the stubborn old guards and the feelings of the radical party. The inventor is of course a genius, and those who use it to promote fighting Japan or fighting Britain can also be said to have some insight.

The customs of the Song Dynasty were probably better than those of China today. In May of the fourth year of Shaoxing, Wang Juzheng, the scribe of daily life, said: "I have seen that in the prefectures and counties of Liangzhe, there is a custom of 'eating vegetables and serving demons'. Before Fang La, the laws were still lenient, and the custom of serving demons was not very prevalent; after Fang La, the laws became stricter, and the custom of serving demons became even more unstoppable... I have heard that those who serve demons have one or two cunning people in each village, called demon heads, who record the names of the villagers, swear an oath to form a party, do not eat meat,... The people are ignorant and say that if we follow the demons, food will be easier to obtain and things will be easier to achieve, so they believe in the demonic sayings and flock to them."... Of course, its badness can be imagined.

Lu You also had a memorandum discussing the like of evil Taoists: "Since ancient times, the rise of bandits has been due to droughts and famines, forced by cold and hunger, gathering together to attack and plunder. If there are appropriate measures, they can be appeased, and they will certainly not cause great concern to the court. Only evil and illusory people deceive good people in peacetime, form secret connections, and wait for the opportunity to act, then their harm is difficult to predict. I have seen that these people are everywhere. In Huainan, they are called "Two Hui Sons," in Liangzhe, they are called "Muni Sect," in Jiangdong, they are called "Four Fruits," in Jiangxi, they are called "Vajra Chan," and in Fujian, they are called "Ming Sect," "Jiedi Zhai," and so on. The names are different, and the Ming Sect is especially prevalent. Even scholars, officials, and soldiers have passed on and practiced it. Their god is called "Ming Envoy," and there are also meat Buddhas, bone Buddhas, blood Buddhas, etc. They wear white clothes and black hats, forming societies everywhere, distributing false scriptures and demonic images carved on woodblocks, using ancestral worship as "ghost summoning," permanently cutting off blood sacrifices, using drowning as holy water for bathing, and other demonic practices are difficult to enumerate. They are closely connected, like glue, and if they steal, it would be terrifying..."

As long as you pay a little attention to observing modern social customs and habits, you will know that the current situation is worse than this; what can be said of vagrants who have no food to eat and no education!

Scientific Spirit Medium 310

— A Slight Criticism

Chinese people admire superstition; at the same time, they like to talk about science with a dark lantern. Therefore, by adding the words "scientific" to the words "spirit medium," it can spread quickly and become popular for a while!

"Sincerity brings spirit," people who have played "spirit medium" generally say: "As long as you are sincere, you can invite any ghost or god, and you can ask about anything, and it is very effective." I have to believe this, and they will certainly not deceive me, but they have been deceived by the inventor of "scientific spirit medium."

Whether there are things like "ghosts and gods" in the world, as people generally imagine, I am ashamed to say that my knowledge is shallow and my experience is insufficient, making it difficult to know. But even if there are, I don't think a plate can invite them. Now, if there are tens of thousands of people, who simultaneously "trouble the plate fairy to invite someone to come and talk," if they can be invited, then the person being invited must have tens of millions of incarnations. Then the world would be full of ghosts and gods. If they cannot be invited, then it is that the "spirit medium" is not "spiritual."

The reason why "scientific spirit medium" is believed in by people is mostly due to curiosity, but also driven by a speculative mentality. Recently, various speculative businesses have been prevalent. The stock exchange can make people rich in a day, and an aviation lottery ticket is worth 500,000 yuan; and ghosts and gods are all-knowing and all-knowing. Just trouble the "plate fairy" to invite them, and with the labor of three people raising their hands and pressing their fingers, the stock exchange market and the first prize number can be predicted, wouldn't that be cheap. But if we think carefully, if the "spirit medium" is "spiritual," then everyone can speculate and make profits, and win the first prize. Do you believe that there will be such a thing in the world?

Science uses real evidence to explain things; saying yes is yes, and saying no is no. Moreover, it can be verified anytime and anywhere and will not be wrong. If it is said that the spirit medium has a scientific basis, then it should also be verifiable anytime and anywhere and will not be ineffective. But as mentioned above, can the spirit medium be effective everywhere?

Perhaps some people will say: How can the spirit medium be ineffective? If it is ineffective, how can the plate move? How can it find the words to answer people's questions? We can use scientific principles to explain this without resorting to ghosts and gods.

"Scientific spirit medium" is the same trick as the planchette that our boring literati play, and the invitation of Zigu that women play in their boudoirs. It is especially similar to the so-called "magic pendulum" of ancient Westerners. (There are many other similar tricks.) Everyone knows planchette, and sometimes it can write a few words on the sand table and make a few articles to answer people's questions. To invite Zigu, two people hold a rice sieve or a rice-washing basket, waiting for it to move on its own, and the number of times it moves can also be used to answer people's questions. A magic pendulum uses a string with a ring or a small ball hanging below. The other end of the string is held between two fingers, and the hand rests on the table to prevent it from shaking. After holding it like this for a while, the string can swing on its own and can also rotate. If a cup is placed next to the magic pendulum and the magic pendulum is asked "what time is it now," it will automatically strike the cup, striking as many times as the clock strikes. If the twenty-six letters of the alphabet are arranged around the magic pendulum and various questions are asked to the magic pendulum, the pendulum can point to each letter in turn, spelling out sentences to answer. This is the same as how the spirit medium's plate can point out the Chinese characters on the word board to answer. Chinese people will naturally say that ghosts and gods have descended, and ancient Westerners often borrowed from God.

In fact, according to the explanation in psychology today, this phenomenon is completely due to "automatic action". It turns out that no matter what thoughts we have in our hearts, we inevitably reveal them unconsciously in our bodies and express them as actions, which is called automatic action. The driving force is transmitted to the planchette stick, magic pendulum, or spirit medium plate, so that the stick, pendulum, or plate also starts to move on its own. And it often corresponds to the thoughts in the heart. Therefore, the reason why the planchette stick, magic pendulum, and spirit medium plate can move is still due to the automatic action of human hands. If it does not borrow from human hands, human thoughts cannot be conveyed, and the stick, pendulum, or plate will never move.

But perhaps some people will argue that the person holding the planchette, the person holding the pendulum, and the person pressing the plate have no thoughts in their minds when holding, holding, or pressing, and are even completely unconscious. Sometimes, when they want it to move, it doesn't move, and when it moves, they want it to stop, but it doesn't stop. It can be seen that this is definitely not stimulated by thoughts.

It should be known that human mental activity is divided into two types: conscious and unconscious. When thinking and acting, if one feels it, that is conscious thinking and acting. If there are thoughts and actions, but one does not feel them, then it is called unconscious thinking and acting. Usually, people's mental activity is conscious, so one is aware of every thought and action. But in addition to this conscious activity, there is also a kind of latent mental activity that does not openly manifest in peacetime, but can also think, perceive, and command the body, just like conscious activity. This mental activity is called subconsciousness in psychology. It does not communicate with conscious activity in peacetime and is completely unconscious. The reason why the person holding the planchette, the person holding the pendulum, and the person pressing the plate are unconscious of their movement is that they are being directed by the subconscious. The reason why they answer people's questions is also that the subconscious is thinking and answering there, so they cannot be conscious of it themselves.

The perception of the subconscious is sometimes very sharp. There are many things that the conscious cannot perceive, but the subconscious can perceive. It knows things that the conscious has never understood. There are many examples of this in psychology. This will not be repeated here. Sometimes the words obtained from planchette are higher than the conscious knowledge of the person holding the planchette; and the words on the "spirit medium" diagram that are not easily found by others are quickly pointed out by the person pressing the plate. This is the reason.

However, even if the subconscious activity is sensitive, it must still be based on past experience. When encountering things that have never been experienced in one's life, there is no way to answer. Even if one answers, it will not be accurate. Therefore, if one asks the person holding the planchette about their future situation, it is often inexplicable. At this time, they can only talk nonsense and deceive themselves and others.

If there are people who believe in "scientific spirit medium," please try to ask any future things and see how accurate they can be!

Recollections 311

— Gao Bi

| Written in Memory of the Third Anniversary of the Death of My Old Friend Chen Xingshu |

(5) One summer, I and a teacher gathered a few like-minded "comrades" to organize a simple reading group - in name a reading group, but in reality it was for escaping the summer heat - using the empty rooms of a school during the summer vacation, and began our "cooperative study" life. Among the several "comrades," there was the suave and refined Sha Landa, the elegant poet Yu Taiyong, the comical and witty Ge Yulei, and the quick-witted and resourceful Chen Xingshu. This gathering was lively enough. Every day, in addition to the two hours of prescribed time, we followed our teacher's guidance and each read some thread-bound books in the room. The rest of the time was mostly spent sitting around and talking. A cup of fragrant tea, a few cigarettes, tasted extremely delicious, and in this way, we dispelled the harassment of the heat demon. The basic purpose of our conversations, although not conflicting, often led to good-natured disputes, and in these disputes, we gained some clever insights. Xingshu was regarded as the embodiment of intelligence. His tone was often extraordinary, whether it was a proposal or a defense, always carrying a leisurely charm that lingered endlessly. He also liked to provide novel additions after others had expounded their ideas, or to offer a turning point when everyone's words deviated from the point. With him, the spirit of our conversations would not be wasted; with him, our little conversation group would never fall into a state of exhaustion.

The school building was located right next to the city wall. We could walk to the top of the wall to take a stroll by using a springboard from the upper floor. Outside the city, there was a very wide river, winding and unfolding. Across the river, there was a teahouse with a waterside pavilion built along the river, which had a unique charm from a distance. Apart from a few scattered shops across the river, the surroundings were all the territory of grass and trees. We would go up to look out over the surroundings in the evening, and our hearts would suddenly open up. The stars adorned our heads, and we heard the croaking of frogs, the murmur of the river, and the rustling of the wind blowing through the grass and trees. The night was silent, and being in it, it was inevitable to cause unwarranted emotion. Xingshu, who was full of emotion, considered this a corner of the world beyond the mundane and often suggested going there.

One day, it was a moonlit night, and we were strolling on the city wall again. Under the silver shroud, everything was dyed with poetry, especially the slightly trembling ripples on the water surface, with the glittering reflections from the moonlight, increasing our aesthetic appreciation. Suddenly, Landa had a new discovery. He asked us to temporarily shrink the scattered gazes around us and direct them to the waterside pavilion across the river. We followed his words as if hypnotized. It turned out that there were several people sitting by the waterside window drinking something in the pavilion. Although we could not tell what kind of liquid they were drinking, we imagined that it should be intoxicating mellow wine. On such a moonlit evening, in such a waterside pavilion, quietly drinking together, what a touching thing of happiness that would be. What was unfolding before us was like a painting, and so each of us could not help but feel a deep sense of melancholy.

"Taiyong must have smelled the aroma of wine from across the river! I think he's blankly lost in thought. Rather than thinking that he was captivated by the entire painting, it would be better to say that the mere cup in front of him stirred up his longing." The mischievous Yulei glanced sideways at me, saying Taiyong, with the intention of waving five strings and watching the flying goose depart. It turned out that both I and Taiyong had a fondness for drinking. But when he said this, he not only intended to tease, but also to break the silence before our eyes. Xingshu finally came to add his opinion:

"Let's not neglect our own position. We, who are here with empty envy, may not be able to understand the true feelings of those who are actually enjoying it. If we were in their place, it would be the same. Reality is disappointing, and the line of imagination is a fulfilling harvest. The pleasure of the idea is just a kind of enticement, visible in front of you, but suddenly behind you, floating and elusive. No matter how you seek and pursue it, it will always maintain a considerable distance." Xingshu's words often contained philosophical components, and were not entirely a kind of self-deprecating language like "sour grapes."

Corpse 313

— Zhang Yiping

Plum rain season. The gray sky, without a trace of rain, the weather is more terrifyingly muggy and hot than in June. A'gen from the Fuxing Tea Garden had just finished scrubbing the planks and was using an iron rod to stoke his coal stove. He was barefoot, his trouser legs rolled up to his calves, revealing rather sturdy calves, his upper body covered with a short jacket. He bent his legs, his eyes narrowed into slits, watching the flames in the coal stove. This was the most important task of his every morning, his food, lodging, wife, and children seemed to be rolling on these flames.

The water in the kettle was bubbling and hissing as if gasping for breath. A'gen sighed in relief, picked out the half-smoked cigarette butt from behind his ear, struck a match, and sat down on the stool, resting his muddy feet. A group of villagers carrying vegetables walked past the door, heading to the vegetable market. A'gen tossed away the cigarette butt, guessing that it was almost time for Grandpa Xu to arrive. There was a sound of clearing phlegm outside the door, it was indeed that tall Grandpa Xu. A'gen slapped the stool and jumped up, almost tripping over something under his feet. Muttering to himself, he loudly greeted Grandpa Xu.

The person called Grandpa Xu did not immediately respond. He wiped the sweat from his forehead with a handkerchief, carefully walked to his usual seat, placed the paper package in his hand on the corner of the table, bent down to tidy up his trouser leg ties, and when he raised his head, his nose and upper lip were twisted together.

"A'gen, what's that stinky smell?" he said loudly.

"Um, Grandpa Xu," the one who had just lifted the kettle quickly turned around. "Grandpa Xu, the sewer was clogged last night, and it hasn't been cleared yet today, that stinky smell…" He deliberately twisted his nose a few times, "(Once you get used to it, it's nothing…)" He didn't pay attention to the other party's reaction, and laughed to himself.

Then, silence.

Only then did A'gen boldly take the teapot and approach Grandpa Xu's table, pouring a full cup, quietly standing aside waiting for Grandpa Xu's words, which had not changed for years: "A'gen, go get three sesame cakes."

Not today, Grandpa Xu forgot, he must be hungry, A'gen couldn't help but say:

"Grandpa Xu, would you like some snacks?"

Grandpa Xu did not answer, it seemed that everything had changed today. He slowly raised the teacup, brought it to his lips, then stopped. After a long while, he suddenly turned his head towards A'gen.

"A'gen, do you know?"

Like a thunderbolt, the other person retreated three steps as if avoiding a slap, his copper-bell eyes wide open. A'gen didn't know anything.

"Zhu Xiaoquan is dead." His fist struck the table, probably because of the plum rain season, the sound wasn't crisp. "Heaven has no eyes!"

"Grandpa Zhu…" He jumped forward like lightning, tripping again, but A'gen didn't mutter, and also forgot his reason for being, sitting on Grandpa Xu's side. "Grandpa Zhu is dead?"

Grandpa Xu stared at the teacup, closed his mouth, and started playing coy. A'gen wanted to reach out and push Grandpa Xu a few times. "Which Grandpa Zhu?! Didn't he get two big silver dollars for the Dragon Boat Festival? Grandpa Zhu's death is like losing my wife and children…" Grandpa Xu finally spoke:

"A'gen, go get three sesame cakes!"

Disappointed, A'gen took the money. Two customers shouted in from the front: "Zhu Xiaoquan is dead!" A'gen felt like he had been sentenced to death: two dollars, two dollars, wishing him wealth and fortune on the first day of the New Year, hmph! It's all for nothing, heaven has no eyes! He forgot to call Grandpa Wang and Grandpa Wang Er inside to invite them in, and went out on his own.

Northeastern Compatriots Will Never Forget They Are Chinese 314

— Meng Ruo

Not long ago, a certain important diplomatic figure expressed his opinion on the Northeast issue, saying a few words like this: "My opinion on the Northeast issue is that it is impossible to recover the four northeastern provinces by force, and it is also difficult to do so through diplomacy. Therefore, our main task now is to ensure that the people of the Northeast do not forget that they are Chinese, because the decline of national consciousness is the most terrible thing. If the people of the Northeast cannot retain their national consciousness, then over time, there will be no way…"

Our view is exactly the opposite. We believe that to save the Northeast, the most important thing is not to make the people of the Northeast not forget that they are Chinese, but to make the Chinese people not forget that the Northeastern compatriots are also Chinese. Why? The Northeastern compatriots have been trampled under the iron hooves of the Japanese for nearly three years, suffering the tragedy of losing their provinces and homes. Except for a very small number of people who are obsessed with power and profit, willing to be slaves and willing to be lackeys of the Japanese, the general public, since the September 18th Incident, how have they been longing for the motherland, how have they been hoping for the government to send troops to recover the lost land, how have they been organizing volunteer armies to fight against the Japanese? Is there still any need to worry that they will forget that they are Chinese? On the contrary, our compatriots inside the customs, seeing the fleshy dancers and movie stars every day, and their personal rights and happiness, may not have time to think about the Northeastern compatriots also being Chinese.

Look, the Northeastern compatriots have recently secretly sent a (Letter to the Elders of the Country). The letter recounts the pain of being in a conquered land, earnestly encouraging the motherland to strive and revitalize itself, to resist foreign aggression together, and to avoid following the same path as the Northeast. It also earnestly hopes that the motherland will unite from top to bottom and prepare in advance for the recovery of the lost land. The words are sad and the feelings are sincere, every word a tear, making it heartbreaking to read!

They also cite Italy, Russia, and Germany ten years ago as examples, hoping that the elders of the motherland (quickly prepare and secretly organize), as a (better late than never) plan. They believe that (if our elders can abandon the prejudices of individualism and temporarily adopt a unified attitude towards foreign countries, heaven helps those who help themselves, and victory will surely be achieved.) However, they (do not merely rely on the elders and willingly endure slavery).

Finally, they also say (Those of us who are forced by life to stay in the Northeast, or who serve in the so-called Manchukuo, should not all be regarded as traitors, because most of them still try their best to repay the Han people. This must be understood. Moreover, at the very least, the country should not regard them as sparrows to be driven away. Therefore, among the Northeastern people now living inside the customs, some are our fathers and brothers, some are our sons and younger brothers, wandering like lost dogs. Our country and the elders of North China should have pity and comfort them, and not despise and exclude them because they have lost their provinces and homes, making them feel attacked from both inside and outside. This is what we entrust to the elders of the country above all else.)

Alas! Hearing these sad words, what will the people of the country think? I really cannot bear to finish reading it!

Or a Kind of Relief Sculpture 315

— Xi Zhen

Night, the streets of a dead city. When the waiter from the coffee shop, having finished his work at the closed night market, took off his white coat and walked onto the street, carrying legs and eyes tired from work, he looked at the dead artery of the city.

The advertising lights at the entrance of the (Vienna Beauty Salon) were dark. Two dogs sniffed each other next to the closed iron gate. One dog suddenly pounced on the other; it barked, the sound floating sparsely across the street like the ringing of a bell.

Floating;

The patrolman with the hand lantern standing on the corner, the closed iron gates of the shops, the black display windows, the red alarm bell at the entrance of the pharmacy.

Looking and looking, angrily, dragging his heavy, exhausted legs, Luotinov thought again; (Has this world really died?)

A hot wind was blowing, and the five-kopeck worth of alcohol was taking effect in his brain: dragging his heavy, exhausted legs, and also dragging his heavy, exhausted eyes; (Nocturnal fantasy.)

(He remembered; Peter Keller's Spanish-style residence, the garden with Italian roses, the Sunday night banquet, his grandfather's military uniform with gold stars, his father's dashing gentlemanly demeanor, his own youth built on the heads of others, his young wife, hanging on the arms of American sailors every night, calling (darling), empty boxes of cotton wool and (Kotex), the strong smell of five-kopeck worth of alcohol, wearing the only pair of military trousers from the Czarist era, patched more than a dozen times, and three buttons missing.)

(The glory of the Czar!)

As the chemical reaction of the alcohol was taking place, he almost shouted it out loud; but no, looking at the patrolman's hand lantern on the corner, he suppressed the great outburst that had risen to his lips, what came out was a distorted tone;

(Damn, damn dog things.)

Dragging his legs, he walked to the tightly closed, pitch-black door of an (Apteka) (Russian for "pharmacy"), looked at the sleeping old watchman, looked at his fluffy white beard, pushed him awake, fixed his red eyes on his face, and spat out unclear noises; (Tell me, old man, where has the glory of the Czar gone? Where is our golden laughter? When will it come back? You tell me, you tell me!)

Shaking his fluffy white beard, spit splashing onto his face; (Get out of here, you wild dog! Who knows? Who knows? Aren't I the same as you?)

(Damn old dog! I'll beat you to death;) He clenched his fist with bulging veins, swung, missed, and then dragged his legs away. Astonished;

(Politeness? Gentleness? The elegance of saying (Yes, sir; that's right, very true)? The soft tone of saying (Farewell, miss), (Please help yourself, madam) to women?)

It's changed, everything has changed. Now they say; (Damn, killable dog things!)

But that's not right, didn't they often say (dog things) before too?

Leaning against the wall, he closed his heavy red eyes.

In the distance, he heard the large clock in the watch shop strike five times. Milk carts were passing on the street, bicycles delivering morning newspapers, and large trucks watering the streets. The patrolmen all went back to report for duty, carrying their hand lanterns; the ones who replaced them were all clusters of (Sigang) wearing steel vests, the buttons on their pistol pouches were open; the prisoner van drove out of the police station and roamed aimlessly around, the noisy areas, the deserted areas.

He suddenly remembered; (Tomorrow is May)

He heard people say: May is the season for plums

Plum Season 316

— You Qi

| Want some! Sugared plums, ten cents for one!

Round and green, lying in that bamboo basket, coated with a layer of white sugar syrup, the color grayish.

This voice, very bright, shouted from the street into this quiet alley. Whether it was that my nerves were a bit too sensitive, or my hearing was a bit off, when that loud voice floated past my ear, I always felt that it contained an element of sadness.

Page 20

Yes, sadness always has some bitterness for the hearts of wanderers. Moreover, this wave of sadness, today two years ago, had a sad event that I cannot forget?

Indeed, time passes too quickly, this event, in the blink of an eye, is almost three years ago.

It is said that in the course of life, there are indispensable conditions, and love is the main one among these conditions. Because (women) are fascinating, regardless of whether the degree of (fascination) is high or low, and it is very obvious that men are willing to be fascinated. The reason, it is said, is that (women) are an indispensable life element in life.

However, who cares? How much sadness, decay, and even sacrifice has this life element caused!

Mano, is just another member who has embarked on the last journey in this abyss of ups and downs.

People, after all, are emotional animals. In times of ice and fire, they can be angry and hate, and in another turn, they can also be unrestrained and heroic.

If we compare it to Mano, then, the second item never existed between him and Xiu since they met. What could exist was only mutual unrestraint.

I remember that it was not long after they met, a late spring day, in Jiangnan, when the grass was growing: green sky, green grass, green suburbs, green treetops, in short, this was the season for young men and women to be intoxicated.

It seemed to be a Sunday? We walked together on the quiet Yuyuan Road. The road surface was strangely flat, and the houses were so magnificent! Walking, walking, underfoot, although there were no leather shoes, the rhythm was very harmonious. The warm wind blew on people's faces, kissing away a trace of lighthearted smile.

Walking into Zhaofeng Park, I couldn't help but feel a little lost. Look, in that green lawn, under that umbrella-shaped cypress tree, beside that mountain stone stream, on that secluded walkway, isn't it? Pairs of couples were walking very slowly, talking, the tone so gentle! Although there were obvious differences in race, there was no difference in mood. Occasionally, I glanced at Mano, who said that he didn't have the same happiness as them!

Perhaps, the mood of a wanderer is always lonely and bitter. At that time, I instinctively felt a component of sadness. I couldn't say why, but there was absolutely no jealousy in it. I don't know why, I always fantasized, I always thought that the mood in front of me would not last long, at most, it would only be like a cloud of smoke, in the blink of an eye, it would run away.

In the autumn of that year, they traveled to Hangzhou together. What happened after that, I never received a letter from them.

丨丨Perhaps they have already cohabited? Maybe they have already broken up! Who can be sure, but a letter should have come? In idle moments, I often think like this.

Friends, when they are together, they gradually become closer, and after they leave, they will slowly fade away.

Here, the shadows of Mano and Xiu were forgotten in my memory.

The harsh winter unknowingly slipped past, and when the swallows flew to Jiangnan, they brought such a message:

………After Mano and Xiu returned, although they struggled hard and wanted to fulfill their wishes, they were eventually forced by their parents more and more urgently, and they had no economic ability to be independent. Therefore, they jointly committed suicide by taking poison a few days ago, leaving a suicide note, and their relatives and friends were all weeping………

After reading it, I didn't feel particularly sad, only that loneliness and sadness had added a thicker layer of sadness.

This time, my wandering soul wandered back from outside again. I don't know what gust of wind directed me to step on the quiet Yuyuan Road again. Ah, everything is still the same, but where is Mano? Where is Xiu? Where is the harmonious rhythm underfoot? They will never be seen again.

With great difficulty, I walked to a street corner, a boy was carrying a bamboo basket and shouting 丨丨Want some, sugared plums, ten cents for one!

When the sharp voice floated past my ear, a burst of sadness rushed into my heart!

Xie San 317

— Bu Wei

Speaking of Xie San, people immediately think of a tenant farmer in his sixties, with a bent back and a protruding belly, and a face that always looked very sad.

Every time the east turned white, he was already up, without even washing his face, walking to the employer's house to do odd jobs. For the price of five cents, he had to shed sweat and blood all day, from dawn to dusk.

The fields that he cultivated himself were all planted at night after he finished his odd jobs, always working past midnight every night.

Years of drought, the fields were cracked by the sun. Every farmer wore a mourning face, and the old farmer Xie San was naturally one of them, because he was also one of the tenant farmers.

The hot June passed, followed by the arrival of the cool autumn, which was the time for the landlords to collect rent. At Xie San's house, Wang Er Ye (his landlord) also sent his accountant to urge the rent.

Xie San said many good things to Mr. Li (Wang Er Ye's accountant), giving all the twenty-odd stone of grain in his home to Wang Er Ye, and promising to pay Wang Er Ye's rent with the money he earned from doing odd jobs by the New Year, only then did he get Mr. Li's permission and was not arrested and sent to prison by the police.

Xie San's family now had nothing to eat! They were often seen eating vegetables as a meal, and when the vegetables were finished, they ate grass; when the grass was finished, they ate tree roots; although they lived like this, his family did not starve to death after all.

The harsh winter returned to the world again, and Xie San was now beginning to collect his wages.

At night, Xie San looked at the wages he had collected 丨copper coins and silver dollars, stunned, unable to hold back two lines of hot tears, which burst out of his eyes: The few coins he had earned with blood and sweat for a year were about to be transferred to Wang Er Ye's hands again.

Since the great drought that year, there had been several years of great harvests: although the grain prices were very low, having such a good harvest, he could still sell some for money. Xie San's family did not have to worry about not having anything to eat; a trace of a smile appeared on Xie San's face for the first time.

After years of living like a cow or a horse, he now actually had more than one hundred yuan in savings, which he and his son had accumulated from doing odd jobs and selling grain.

Bandits were spreading everywhere! In order to avoid bandits interfering with his fields, Wang Er Ye sold his land cheaply.

The hope was burning in Xie San's mind; At night, Xie San tossed and turned, thinking, and finally decided to buy Wang Er Ye's fields; this was truly a world turned upside down, a tenant farmer buying the landlord's fields!

After eating lunch, Xie San put on his only half-new blue cotton cloth gown, double-nose carp shoes, coarse cloth white socks, and happily walked to Wang Er Ye's house to buy Wang Er Ye's fields.

Wang Er Ye now decided to sell the seventeen mu of fields on the side of the road to Xie San, and at a price of five yuan per mu. Xie San was transformed from a tenant farmer into a half-self-cultivating farmer. How happy he was!

The army came to the countryside to (suppress bandits)! In order to facilitate (bandit suppression) and the transportation of guns and ammunition, the long-distance bus route was under construction.

Unfortunately, the location of Xie San's field was right on the path that the bus had to take, and therefore it was leveled.

The unfortunate news immediately spread throughout the village! (Luckily I sold that field to Xie San, otherwise I would have been really unlucky!) A smug sneer flashed across Wang Er Ye's face.
