A Ray of White Light 319

— Ma Ying

A friend from Hangzhou reported to me: (During the Shambala Mandala Dharma Assembly photography, the magnesium flash suddenly exploded, a ray of white light, running like a flying rainbow, the Living Buddha was actually frightened and stepped down from his seat.) Having already become a Buddha, he still fears white light like a tiger, not only changing color, but actually stepping down from the altar, is this not strange beyond strange. So after hearing this news, I was puzzled all day, thinking until my brain swelled, and then I suddenly realized.

The Shambala Mandala Assembly is held, firstly, to pray for peace, and secondly, to recommend the deceased and prolong life. If the world were truly peaceful through prayer, then the demon of war would abandon his armor and weapons and flee, and heroes would have no place to use their strength. If the general wandering souls were able to ascend to heaven and be reincarnated through transcendence, then King Yama would definitely have to reduce a sum of income. Therefore, the Living Buddha knew that by doing this Dharma service, although he could bestow grace upon countless sentient beings, he would also incur resentment from several villains. If there were grievances, they would surely be repaid, and if there were grudges, they would surely be avenged. The Living Buddha knew that they would not be willing to give up, so he was constantly on guard.

Sure enough, on the day of the photography, a white light flew over. The Living Buddha suddenly remembered the sword immortals and swordsmen in the old novels, whose killing weapon was white light; perhaps this white light was the flying knife or flying sword released by the assassins hired by his enemies. Because the Living Buddha was alive, he was not yet able to hide or escape, or even point his finger and spit out a lotus flower of five colors to block the path of the white light, so he could only run away to avoid it.

However, after being frightened, the Living Buddha did not change his original intention and continued to use his magical powers to continue praying, showing the Living Buddha's indomitable spirit. In the future, the world will be peaceful and the population will increase, all thanks to the Living Buddha. After the common people have benefited and the deceased souls have kowtowed in gratitude, everyone should put their palms together and respectfully express their thanks, saying: (Suddenly, a white light, running like a flying rainbow. The Living Buddha paled and fled in fear. Thanks to the blessing of Heaven, the white light was extinguished. The little devils in hell, all ascended to heaven; the human world is at peace, the country is prosperous and the people are safe. The Buddha's grace is spread in all directions! The Buddha's virtue is as high as the sky and as long as the water!

Eating and Love 320

— A Skinny Person

Which is more important, unemployment or heartbreak? This question has been debated before. Ultimately, is eating more crucial, or is love? This is a very interesting question. In my opinion, eating and love should not be separated. That is to say, this question should not be viewed as two separate issues. Rather, these two issues should be discussed together.

Eating and love may seem like two different things, but in reality, they are one and the same: "life." Life includes eating, and at the same time, it also includes love. Therefore, the conclusion should be: "If you have food to eat, you have love to pursue." Eating and love are forever linked together. If you have food to eat, you have love to pursue; conversely, if you have no love to pursue, you will inevitably have no food to eat. This is the unity of eating and love in life. Needless to say in ancient societies, but especially in modern society, this theory is proven to be correct. Because in a society dominated by money and power, everything becomes a commodity, and people also become commodities, especially women, who are the most commodified of commodities. In this commodity society, as long as you have money, anyone can buy anyone else. Women, in particular, have become objects of trade in the market. In this way, love is combined with eating and cannot be separated. Whoever can afford to eat can afford a woman—that is, whoever can obtain love. The greater the ability to buy food, the greater the ability to buy women—that is, the easier it is to find love. Conversely, those who have no food to eat cannot buy women—that is, they cannot find love at all. In fact, love and eating have become one and the same. The conclusion derived from the fact that love and eating are one and the same is that there is no distinction between the importance of unemployment and heartbreak. Unemployment means having no money to buy food, while heartbreak means having no money to buy a woman. They seem like two different things, but they are actually the same problem. As long as you have money, you can buy both at the same time. The core of the problem is not about unemployment or heartbreak, but about having money or not having money. With money, all problems can be solved; without money, everything becomes a problem. This is the core of modern society. The core of modern society is money. Money dominates all of humanity and determines all social problems. In modern society, unemployment and heartbreak are merely various secondary phenomena derived from this central problem. Disregarding the central problem and seeking solutions solely from these secondary problems will not yield any answers. Then, why is money the central problem that dominates everything in modern society? This is because in modern society, money is separated from the masses. Wealth is originally meant to be shared by all of humanity, but now a portion of people have locked up this wealth, creating a vast distance between the majority of people and wealth. This is how money is able to dominate all of human life. Money dominates humanity, and as a result, humanity cannot dominate wealth and is, in fact, enslaved by wealth. Because people are slaves to wealth, all problems cannot be solved without money. Money replaces the central position of all problems. To achieve satisfactory solutions to all problems, we must first reverse the social order in which people are dominated by money and transform it into a social order in which money is dominated by people. This is the central point of solving the problem.

Amateur Mailbox

Scientific Spirit Writing 321

Editor:

Recently, a type of "Scientific Spirit Writing Chart" has become popular in the market. It was invented by Bai Tongjun, a Chinese student who studied in Germany, and sells for one and a half dollars. It is widely purchased, and almost every student, large or small, and every family has one. I also bought one and studied it carefully. I also feel that it is very accurate. It can summon Sun Yat-sen and others. I wonder if it is a psychological effect or if there is a scientific basis? Now, some ignorant women are using it to ask about lottery numbers and gambling tickets. As soon as they ask for what number will be drawn, they use a lot of money to bet on it. If they lose, some even want to die. This is an important social problem. Please gather experts to study it together and provide a detailed response. I wish you good health. Sincerely, Li Taosheng, a reader.

Answer: The editor has recently seen these so-called "Scientific Spirit Writing Charts" hung on stalls by the roadside when traveling on the main roads. I am very familiar with these kinds of "spirit writing" things, so even though it bears the name "scientific," it does not arouse my curiosity enough to take a look at it. After receiving your letter, to learn its content, I bought one to see what it was all about. After looking at it, I couldn't help but laugh. This thing is indeed more advanced than the old-fashioned planchette writing, and its methods of deception are also more clever. In fact, this kind of spirit writing has no profound or mysterious principles at all. We can expose the true face of this "Ouija board" with just common sense. Three people use their middle fingers to press on the bottom of the planchette. After several tens of minutes, wouldn't your hands be numb and sore? Once your hands are numb, they will inevitably tremble involuntarily, so you will feel that the "spirit" has truly summoned a "ghost" (?) for you. Moreover, when three fingers are placed on the planchette, the force cannot be evenly distributed. If one person applies slightly more force, the planchette will inevitably move. The other two people, seeing the planchette move, will inevitably follow its movement, but if they follow its movement without applying any pushing force in the direction of the planchette's movement, their fingers will lift off the planchette. Therefore, the other two people will then involuntarily push the planchette. After that, the ratio of the force applied by the three people will become even more uneven, and the planchette's path will naturally become even more irregular, spinning around and around. This is the origin of the "spirit summoning someone to come and talk."

As for its accuracy, it can be accurate to the extreme. If you ask who is coming, you must already have an answer in your mind and you must be looking for the letters of the visitor's name on the chart. In this way, even if you don't intentionally push it, because of what you see with your eyes, you will inevitably and naturally make the "planchette" find it for you. I remember when I was learning to ride a bicycle as a child, I saw a small car parked nearby and wanted to avoid it, but I still ended up hitting the small car and falling over. This is possible when your hand is sore and trembling. Moreover, there are many Chinese characters with the same sound but different meanings, making it even easier to force an association. I think, apart from these two factors and intentionally assisting the "spirit," there is absolutely no other reason for its "accuracy." If it is not "accurate," if the answer is not what you asked, or if the answer is unintelligible, then you will inevitably blame it on the insincerity of yourself or the other two people, because only sincerity brings accuracy. Insincerity, of course, cannot bring accuracy. In other words, spirit writing is still about being "accurate" with sincerity. I'm afraid it's very difficult to achieve "sincerity." If the "spirit" has the slightest doubt, it's insincere; if you have any distracting thoughts, it's insincere; if you don't pray hard enough to the person being summoned, it's insincere... and so on. There will never be a time of "sincerity." The so-called mystery of "scientific spirit writing" lies in this. But I say it is more advanced than the old-fashioned planchette writing for a reason. The old-fashioned one requires writing out the "characters." It won't be accurate unless you cheat, but this one doesn't need to. The old-fashioned one requires two people to stand opposite each other and hold the planchette stick, making it easy to balance the force. If one side doesn't intentionally apply force, it is difficult to move it, while this one only requires pressing the bottom of the planchette with your fingers, making it easier for your hands to become sore and for it to move. So the components of "accuracy" are much greater than in the old-fashioned one. As for what you said about ignorant women using it to ask about gambling, that's not surprising at all. This kind of spirit writing is produced because of the development of gambling and speculative psychology in society. No matter which superstitious person, they rarely have their fortune told when they are successful. But when they are unsuccessful, they ask for fortune sticks and calculate the hexagrams every day. This is a certain pattern. In this year of economic panic and increased unemployment, it is very difficult to get rich except through gambling. So the rich gamble on government bonds, and the poor gamble on flower associations. The only way to get rich is to gamble. Gambling is completely dependent on so-called "fate" and "chance," which cannot be controlled by people's consciousness. The winning number of the aviation lottery can only be known by heaven before it is drawn. Ghosts and gods can tell you. Therefore, so-called scientific spirit writing can be the only guide for gamblers. You can see that there are fewer scientific spirit writing charts on the market now. The reason is that the aviation lottery has already been drawn, the winning number has already been shaken out, and there is no need to ask the "spirit" anymore. So, it's not surprising that these practices of seeking gods and asking for divination are so popular. This is precisely the psychological manifestation of most people being filled with "finding no possible way out but having to rely on fate." If people can know the proper ways to make a living, this kind of trick will inevitably disappear. Conversely, even if scientific spirit writing charts are defeated, similar kinds of spirit writing things will continue to emerge endlessly. And therefore, our only way to defeat seeking gods and asking for divination is to make people realize the direction they should strive in, and to have a firm belief in this direction. — Editor

Fiction

MADAM X (1) 322

— Zhang Yiping

Friday, March 30th. A calendar with chromium numerals lay on the manager's oiled desk. Two young debt collectors, city-slickers, held their Stetson hats in their hands, presenting four Chinese bank checks for 1,500 yuan, due the next day.

The manager of the World Trading Company, a handsome man with Chaplin hair, Cowlman eyes, a Hepplewhite nose and mouth, was a narcissistic dandy. Raising his exquisite fingers, he removed the cigar from his lips, flicked off the ashes, casually pulled over a hardcover ledger, filled in four entries of 1,500 yuan, and slightly nodded his head, as if wary of his Chaplin hair falling down. The young debt collectors retreated to their positions.

As the clock struck five, the office boy handed over a letter from the Yangtse Hotel just as he was pulling out the safe key from his beige suit.

Cowlman's eyes fixed on the handwriting on the envelope. He frowned as if lost in thought, and awkwardly tore open the envelope.

Minson:

We arrived in Shanghai today, staying at room 356 of the Yangtse Hotel. Please come for a chat at your earliest convenience, and also to meet my new wife.

Yours sincerely, Junyang. Today

A Hepplewhite-like smile appeared. Before his eyes seemed to float the image of Junyang: "I'm heartbroken... I want revenge! A beautiful girl is waiting for me in Peiping, Minson, goodbye! I'm alone, never stepping onto Shanghai's Bund again?" He waved his hand, looking pitiful. Three years, without a single word. And now he brings back a new wife, a beautiful girl from Peiping.

Thinking, he snatched the check key and stuffed it into his pocket, swiftly turning to leave the World Trading Company's glass doors. The elevator, as if waiting just for him, descended from the fifth floor and he tumbled into the car parked in front of the door.

... Piled-up hair, a loud red tie, waving his hands, sitting in the coffee shop smoking cigars every day, Junyang, a man who knows nothing of women, needs a woman. That Saturday night in spring: "Who would love a man like you!" Sending him off on the boat to Peiping...

He could not continue to think. The chauffeur opened the door, waiting for him to alight. Smoothing the wrinkles on his knees, he ordered the car to return.

He energetically mounted the stone steps. In the elevator, he raised his exquisite fingers to smooth his Chaplin hair, and gently knocked on the door of room 356.

... Minson, am I heartbroken? He had expected that sentimental voice.

"Is this Mr. Wang? Please come in." Pure Peiping accent. A beautiful wife greeted him at the door.

"Is Mr. Junyang in?" He removed his hat and inquired with gentlemanly courtesy.

"He just went out. He'll be back shortly. Please come in." A Peiping smile. The Peiping girl has fallen in love with Junyang. He strode in, as proud as if entering an office.

The Peiping wife offered cigarettes and tea. They sat down facing each other.

Film Special

The Boldness of American Producers 323

— Luo Fu

Written after viewing "Film: Nana"

An ancient philosopher, when discussing Apollo, said: "Apollo is a god of music, but also a god of archery. I love his songs, but I fear his arrows!" After watching "Film: Nana," the first impression that comes to mind is such a bittersweet association.

If you want to see some aspects of French society during the Third Republic in "Film: Nana," or observe the overlapping life of the actress Nana, as described by the naturalist writer Émile Zola, then your hopes are in vain. Furthermore, if you want to see some of the exposure of the corruption of the aristocratic bourgeoisie or the criticism of social injustice at the time by this writer with a strong sense of justice, then your expectations will be denied. "Film: Nana" and "Novel: Nana" have no blood or hereditary relationship. The original work is merely a suggestion for the film. Samuel Goldwyn, the American film producer, with typical American boldness and disregard for others, unceremoniously seized the "songs" he liked from the works of the French naturalist writer and avoided the "arrows" he feared!

In the words of Georg Brandes, a great critic of Zola's time, "Zola is... a thinker who cannot unlock the profound secrets of the age, an incomplete poet under the standards of aesthetics, but in his talent and dedication, in his fairness and courage, he is fully entitled to be a warrior alongside Taine, Renan, Rousseau, and Voltaire!" In his works, he mercilessly described the ruling class of the time, lashed out at the greed and reaction of the urban and rural merchant classes, exposed the deception and crimes of stockbrokers and religious figures, and further explored the connection between phenomena and causes, pointing to the impending revolution. In Goldwyn's eyes, these were undoubtedly terrifying "arrows," sharp "arrows."

However, on the one hand, Zola was a popular follower of the Lombroso school of determinism. He could not unlock the profound secrets of the age or obtain a necessary vision for the transformation of social organization from his frantically exploring scientific method. He merely borrowed the principles of heredity and environment, which scientists at the time were passionately discussing, and used his astonishingly sincere and meticulous technique to depict all the morbid phenomena of society at that time: splendor, luxury, licentiousness, and morbid beauty. This is the "song" of the naturalist poet, a "song" that can please the well-versed citizens of the fin de siècle and film producers.

Adopting these derivative descriptions and plagiarizing the evocative name "Nana," what emerged under the massive production costs and advertising expenses was a film of "Nana" that washed away all the spicy and filthy "Zolaesque" elements and added some intense "Dumas-esque" sorrow and sentimentality! Indeed, this is an era of war and revolution. The licentious and decadent "Nana" of the 1870s could become a nationalist warrior in the 1940s, listening to the cries of "To Berlin!" outside the window and shouting the slogan "France needs you!" at the moment of death! Is this the work of Zola, famous for the Dreyfus Affair? This is already something "beyond a wry smile."

Apart from Anna Sten's outstanding acting, what can be admired is Samuel Goldwyn's characteristically American bold, audacious production policy and Willard Mack's courageous adaptation.

Audience Opinions

Blood Under the Chastity Arch 324

— Shen Weng

Thoughts after watching "A Good Night"

In this era of transition between old and new, whether a woman who has lost her husband should keep her chastity for him has become a very serious issue. This film, "A Good Night," is produced in the study of this issue. At the beginning of the film, the reel is marked with a few subtitles that say: "There are three things that are plentiful in Bai Village: cypress trees, memorial arches, and widows..." Although it is only a few simple words, it has fully expressed the unbreakable old habits of China for thousands of years, and the main theme of the film is revealed in one sentence.

The central consciousness of this film is undoubtedly to criticize the hypocrisy of chastity. The protagonist of the film is a young woman who yearns for the comfort of love. Unfortunately, her husband dies, and she is asked to live alone. After all, she is not a living dead person and cannot forget the instinct of desire. However, because she is in awe of the power of ethics, she does not dare to restrain herself. When she is silently facing her lover in the countryside, she almost loses control because of the impulse of desire, but the phantoms of the chastity arches suddenly appear in her mind, one after another. She can only wail and run away.

In addition to this, it also describes: the clan chief having secret affairs with married women, but verbally pretending to be benevolent and righteous; the petty tyrant defrauding the weak, and interfering with the freedom of widows because he cannot satisfy his own sexual desires; the old chaste mother is crushed to death under the chastity arch, only to be cursed that she is suffering the consequences of her own actions. All these expose the strange phenomena in remote rural areas, and it can be said to be a thorough exposure.

After Watching "A Good Night" 325

— Lin Chen

In China's century-old feudal society, chastity was regarded as the supreme virtue of women. Under the decaying and majestic chastity arches were buried countless young widows' blood and souls.

The entire consciousness of "A Good Night" is commendable. It uses the spiritual impulses of a young widow and the difficult-to-resolve conflict with old concepts as a backdrop, not only satirizing the hypocrites of false morality, but also boldly exposing the absurdity and cruelty of the old ethics. When the young widow, Yunlin, is pointed at by the crowd and hit with snow, and when Yunlin's mother-in-law unreservedly retorts that these clan chiefs and people are all bullying the weak widows by relying on their power, this climax is very successful and powerfully arouses the audience's anger and sympathy. Therefore, the consciousness of "A Good Night" is very suitable for women in the current transition period, especially female students.

In terms of performance, it generally lacks transitions, so the entire tone is static, but when recalling the psychological description of the widow, one feels its value.

In terms of the story, there seem to be some unreal aspects. According to the old Chinese customs, there is very little punishment for unchaste men, because there is fundamentally no custom of judging men's unchastity. In "A Good Night," there is actually an incident of expelling the twenty-fourth generation descendant. I wonder if there is such a thing?

In terms of technique, I am very satisfied. Yunlin uses well water to look at her face, and her feet move upon hearing the sound of the zither, which systematically expresses the emotions of a young widow. When Yunlin is drying clothes, the memorial arch is moving in her heart. When she is undergoing the "Last Judgment," she is pointed at by the crowd. Snow footprints (imitating "Beauties Taming Tigers"), the clan chief's close-up of his angry face (imitating "Crossroads"), two shadows during the secret meeting, Yunlin hiding behind the tree to see them off, etc., all have unprecedented and beautiful success. Using peach trees as a background adds even more sadness.

Actress Tan Ying is the best. Her movements and expressions are mostly in the slow Western style. But she lacks eye expressions. Jiang Junchao has not made much progress. His expressions are not very suitable for the amorous young master in the play. Tang Tianxi hasn't been seen for a long time, and his style has changed, probably a little stiff. Chen Binyu, who plays A'pei, is somewhat fiery. The rest are mediocre.

Review of "A Good Night" 326

— Guyue

Speaking of the performance of "A Good Night," it can be satisfactory in many ways. This film can always give us some satisfaction.

Yunlin washing rice is the most brilliant scene in the film. She looks at the shadow in the well with great resentment, and when the bucket is lowered, it disperses the resentful shadow piece by piece. The photography is excellent, and the expression is also profound. It can truly portray a widow suppressed under the old ethics, feeling boundless emotion for her youth! Therefore, Yunlin is a very difficult role to play. On the one hand, she cares about her reputation, and on the other hand, she cannot suppress the fire of her youth. Being in this dilemma, she can deal with it calmly, no matter what, it is a success.

Mother Liu is a believer in the old ethics, but she has the courage to expose this darkness, which implies the awakening of humanity. The expression at the time of awakening is quite successful.

Zhu Ying is an elementary school teacher who opposes ethics, but he finally fails! His sincere heart still cannot awaken Yunlin, and finally, this tragedy is reflected.

The photography has two excellent scenes, especially when Yunlin is grinding rice and looking into the well. The photography of the cypress trees and arches in Bai Village is also quite successful.

The director's skills are very high. He can make the distribution of the entire play obtain some very suitable talents. However, the first two scenes, when focusing on Mother Liu, are too roundabout.

The performance of the whole play can be satisfactory, this is the last thing to say. At the same time, it is much better than "The Wind," because "The Wind" only describes a woman who is living in the city, while "A Good Night" describes the entire unfortunate woman.

Amazing News in Two Days 327

— Shen Fen

The fact that Wu Cun of Lianhua has joined Mingxing has become a reality. Now news has come that Gao Zhanfei has joined Mingxing. The contract has been signed with a monthly salary of five hundred yuan, with additional remuneration, and another attached condition, namely that his ranking, apart from Hu Die, is not below other actors.

It is rumored that Cai Chusheng is also wavering and there is talk of joining Mingxing as well.

The Taihua Company, founded jointly by playwright Zuo Mingqian and Bao Zhichao, is currently difficult to realize due to certain reasons. Zuo Ming is currently introduced by a certain gentleman to Tianyi, where he serves as a screenwriter and actor.

Tianyi has established a branch in Hong Kong. Shao Zuiweng specially sent his brother Shao Cunren to Hong Kong to work. It is reported that Cunren has completed discussions with colleagues in the branch company and will return to Shanghai within a few days.

Tianyi's "Dream of the Red Chamber" and "Spring Night Song" will be completed after filming two more large scenes. Chen Yumei will continue to star in "The Graciousness of a Beauty," adapted from Zhang Henshui's novel and scripted by Yu Si, after her starring role in "Dream of the Red Chamber" is completed. The director has been set as Qiu Yixiang.

Mingxing Company has sent people to Hangzhou to film news footage of the Kalachakra Initiation.

Tianyi's document director, Mr. Gao Tianqi, finished writing the "Lotus Picking Song" from "Dream of the Red Chamber" overnight yesterday and returned to his native Shaoxing this morning to visit his family.

Film Novel

Wonder Bar (WonderBar) Five 328

— Uncle Ming

Ines and Harley took the stage. Ines was still entangled with Harley while dancing. Harley, however, showed disgust, scolding her from time to time, and repeatedly throwing her forcefully to the ground. He also cursed at her, saying: (Don't be so weak. Be careful about what you do). Ines was pushed by him and fell. She raised her head and shouted at Harley: (Harley!) Harley said: (Do you still want to be like that?) Ines said: (You, you can't leave me. I won't let you go.) Harley said: (Will you stop talking!) As he spoke, he deliberately executed a difficult step, throwing Ines out again with great force. Ines fell heavily again. Although the audience knew that this was all part of the performance, everyone was so frightened by the realistic expressions that they could barely breathe. Later, Ines said: (Are you going to take Mrs. Leonard with you?) Harley scolded: (What business is it of yours if I take her?) Ines said: (I won't let you take her!) Harley got angry and said: (Oh! You dare to interfere with my affairs!) As he said that, he pushed her hard again, and she fell to the ground. The whole audience stood up in an uproar. Al hurriedly came out to smooth things over, saying: (Everyone, please sit down and relax. This happens every night.) Ines slowly raised her head, and streaks of blood were already flowing from her mouth. She secretly pulled out the dagger from her garter and, following the rhythm of the music, suddenly stood up and went to meet Harley. When they passed each other, she said: (You can't take her away!) She stabbed the knife into Harley's chest. At the same time, the music stopped abruptly with a clang. Al understood what had happened. Harley was still holding Ines in his arms. But he couldn't stand still himself. Applause thundered from all sides. Al rushed over, pretending to congratulate them. He supported Harley and Ines, one arm around each of them. Harley was limp and barely bowed to the audience. The audience cheered again. Al took advantage of the commotion to help them inside.

Harley and Ines entered the dressing room, and Ines immediately fainted. When Al looked at Harley again, he was already dead. In a moment of desperation, Al immediately ran out to find Li Que. He asked Li Que to help him carry Harley's body out before Ines woke up. However, the dance hall was surrounded by police, how could they get out? So they gave a bottle of wine to a policeman outside a small door in advance. The policeman didn't care about anything once he had the wine. Al and Li Que, one on each side, propped up Harley's body, pretending he was drunk, and carried him out. They carried Harley's body all the way to Captain Flynn's car and stuffed him into the trunk. After a while, Captain Flynn came, unaware that there was a dead man in the trunk, so he got into the car and drove away. Before leaving, he even said to Al: (Goodbye, goodbye. Don't forget to buy the newspaper tomorrow.) Al waved to him and said: (Goodbye, Captain. Newspapers? Don't forget, don't forget. You only know half of it.) As he said that, he hurried into the dance hall. He didn't even have time to see Ines, and ran to his own dressing room to put on blackface makeup to perform the black people's dance to paradise. (To be continued)
